Anglo-Egyptian Treaty Concluded, Officially Signed in London on the 27th

Alexandria, Egypt. Negotiations between Egypt and Britain on the conclusion of a new treaty have been underway since March of this year, lasting several months. The clauses concerning military affairs and the Sudan issue have been agreed upon and initialed successively. The clauses on consular jurisdiction have also been agreed upon and initialed this afternoon. Afterwards, a public statement was issued, saying, "The representatives of both sides held a plenary meeting at 7:00 PM today, and all the outstanding clauses in the new Anglo-Egyptian treaty were drafted." With this, the negotiations between the two countries came to an end. Once the Egyptian delegation arrives in London, the official signing ceremony can be held, and the date has been set for the 27th of this month. Egypt will immediately apply to join the League of Nations after the signing. (Havas dispatch from the 12th)

(London) Negotiations between Britain and Egypt on the new treaty have ended, and various clauses have been initialed yesterday. The attention of the newspapers here has now shifted to this matter, and they are not as concerned about the Spanish unrest as they were in the past few days, because Germany and Italy seem to be preparing to negotiate, and the international situation is not expected to cause a crisis for the time being. Among them, the Morning Post published a commentary on the new Anglo-Egyptian treaty, saying, "Since Egypt broke away from British protection and declared independence in 1922, the relationship between Britain and Egypt has been complicated, complex, and very unstable. Now that the delegations of both sides have agreed on a new treaty, the friendly relations between the two countries will surely be strengthened. As for Egypt, the page of Muhammad Ali's reign, which is also a page of the country's struggle for independent sovereignty, has now come to an end, which is not something to celebrate." The newspaper then said, "The Suez Canal is a vital transportation route for the British Empire. If Egypt is the only guardian and is responsible for safeguarding its independence, then the future safety cannot but worry people. Therefore, to say that after the new treaty is concluded, the security of the Empire and Egypt will be established is something that we cannot agree with." (Havas dispatch from the 13th)

Cairo. The Blue Shirt team, a youth group of the Nationalist Party led by Prime Minister Nahas, and the Green Shirt team of the Nationalists have been incompatible for a long time. The members of both sides entered into conflict yesterday in Damanhur when they met on a narrow road. The Green Shirt team accused the Blue Shirt team of receiving foreign subsidies, resulting in a conflict that left one person dead and one injured. (Havas dispatch from the 13th)

China's Trade Surplus with the United States Reaches More Than 1.78 Million US Dollars

(Washington) The Department of Commerce announced today in its international trade report that China's trade surplus with the United States in June reached US$1,789,000. In the six months before June 22, China's trade surplus with the United States totaled US$22,917,000. This statistic further increases the good impression of the United States on the Chinese government's new monetary policy. It is believed here that China's trade surplus can increase exchange credit in the United States, which is a significant sign of currency stability. According to economic experts, China's trade surplus is due to the economic recovery of the United States, which has increased the demand for Chinese goods. In addition, the reduction of Chinese imports is also one of the reasons for this trade surplus. The total value of US exports to China in June was US$5,134,000, while the value in the same period last year was US$2,295,000. The total value of Chinese goods imported by the United States in June was US$6,923,000, while the value in the same period last year was US$4,891,000. In the first six months of this year, US exports to China totaled US$20,990,000, and imports totaled US$43,907,000. Last year, US exports to China totaled US$22,661,000, and imports totaled US$30,341,000. (National Telegram from the 12th)

Serious Situation in Palestine, Arabs Massacre British Soldiers

Jerusalem. Yesterday, ten British soldiers were resting near the Isdraelon Valley, and eight of them were bathing in a small pool. Suddenly, more than 30 Arabs attacked, resulting in the death of one British non-commissioned officer and injuries to three soldiers. At that time, the Arabs were approaching stealthily, first knocking down two sentries, and then opening fire on the soldiers. The British army was caught off guard and did not have time to take up their guns to fight back. The deceased was a corporal. After the Arabs seized the uniforms, guns, and ammunition left by the British soldiers by the pool, they fled into the nearby mountains. A large number of troops and border guards from Transjordan have been dispatched to search the surrounding areas with the help of aircraft. (Reuters dispatch from the 13th)

Center of Spanish Warfare Shifts Again to Near the Portuguese Border, Government Troops Defend Important Town Under Siege, Rebel Giant Planes Bomb

Madrid. Badajoz, the capital of the province of Badajoz near the Portuguese border, has recently been completely surrounded by rebel troops and is expected to fall soon. Although Chiclana, a town in the province of Huelva, is still defended by government troops, the situation is very serious, and it is believed that it will be occupied by the rebel army soon. After a short but fierce battle yesterday, the rebel army defeated the government army and attacked Badajoz. Starting at 4:00 PM, they bombarded the city fiercely and used four three-engine planes to continuously drop bombs on this city, which was as precarious as a pile of eggs. Yesterday, from the top of a small hill on the Portuguese border, it could be seen that the people of Badajoz were fleeing in all directions, and women and children were crossing the international bridge over the Guadiana River into Portuguese territory. The Portuguese border guards were busy inspecting and confiscating weapons, and the men were being detained. A rebel plane dropped a bomb on the refugees crowded on the international bridge trying to cross the river, resulting in about 20 deaths. (Reuters dispatch from the 13th)

Madrid. The war for supremacy in Spain is intensifying, and the decisive battle will not be far away. Although Madrid remains as peaceful as usual, on the northern Guadarrama front, the government is using its superior forces to put pressure on the rebel army led by General Mola. Mola's troops are now moving between Burgos and Zaragoza, trying to hold on. As for the rebel leader General Franco, he has a strong presence in the south, but the rebel forces in the north and south have not yet been able to make contact west of Madrid, because the government forces are now firmly defending Badajoz, and although Franco's planes have repeatedly bombed it, they have not given up. It is said that Franco's troops are now planning to launch an offensive, and there may be a major conflict on the coast near Malaga. Rebel troops and fascists are carrying machine guns and transport vehicles and are advancing to attack the government's main naval base. (Reuters dispatch from the 13th)

Burgos. It has recently been learned that the revolutionary army has made continuous progress in the positions it occupies today. On the northern Guipuzcoa front, the revolutionary army has successively occupied the two cities of Eibar and Villabona. The former is between Tolosa and Zumaya, and although it is a small town, it has an arsenal, and the ammunition needed by the government army in San Sebastian is supplied from here. The latter is six kilometers north of Tolosa. After the revolutionary army obtained these two places, its positions in the Tolosa area were immediately consolidated. Tolosa is a northern industrial center with a population of 10,000 and is the center of Guipuzcoa Province. Now that the area has fallen into the hands of the revolutionary army, San Sebastian has been seriously threatened. As for the southern front, according to news from Seville, the government army in Badajoz has been isolated and will soon surrender to the revolutionary army. The city of Merida to the east has long been occupied by the revolutionary army, so General Franco, commander of the southern front, and General Mola, commander of the northern front, have made contact there. Looking at the overall situation, the provinces and regions currently controlled by the revolutionary army include Galicia, Leon, and Asturias in the northwest, the Extremadura region in the west (except for Badajoz Province), the Andalusia region in the south (except for Malaga and Jaen provinces), Navarre and Old Castile in the north, and Aragon in the northeast, which is more than half of the country. (Havas dispatch from the 12th)

Madrid. In northern Spain, the government army and the rebel army are engaged in a battle for the coastline of San Sebastian and Irun. Tolosa, which was captured by the rebel army, is the throat of San Sebastian and is a strategic location that soldiers must fight for. However, the government army is confident that it will win the final battle and claims that government planes have bombed the rebel barracks and forts in Granada, dropping a total of 10,000 pounds of bombs, and shot down two rebel planes near the city. In addition, 20 bombers have arrived in Madrid, six in Valencia, and four in Catalonia to replenish the government air force. From this, it can be seen that the government army has a good chance of turning defeat into victory in a few days. It is now heard that four bombers are about to bomb the rebel positions in Cordoba, Seville, and Puente Genil. (National Telegram from the 12th)

Spanish Civil War, Both Sides Kill Each Other Miserably, Rebel Army Benefits from Air Transport, Transporting No Fewer Than Twelve Planes of Soldiers Every Day

Madrid. The current military situation in Spain can be summarized as follows: In the most recent period, neither side has been able to occupy a larger city. Although the government army in the north has indeed posed a considerable threat to Zaragoza and Huesca, it is also under considerable pressure from the rebel army in the Irun and San Sebastian areas. At present, two rebel ships have sailed to the above two places to assist in the battle.

Although the government army in southern Spain is currently using guerrilla tactics, there are already signs that General Franco's position is unfavorable. The air force stationed in Seville by General Franco is the most powerful weapon and is now increasing daily. No fewer than twelve planes are transporting troops from Morocco to mainland Spain every day, but the source is unknown. The rebel army transported from Morocco has repeatedly launched surprise attacks in various villages in the south because they are suspected of being loyal to the government, and the killings are very tragic, especially by the Moorish native army. The looting methods they use are extremely terrifying. Anyone who is even slightly suspected will be shot without mercy. Civilians and others who are captured in various villages pay money as the price for the looters to stop their atrocities. The newspapers even publish eulogies to encourage them, such as an editorial in a newspaper edited by a fascist bullfighter in Cordoba, threatening the people who have surrendered to the government, entitled "We will tear their bodies apart like butchering pigs."

At present, illegal incidents are frequently seen in Spain, which is due to the indiscriminate distribution of modern weapons to rude farmers. For example, the government recruited shepherds from the mountains of Granada who were accustomed to throwing stones and taught them how to use hand grenades. (Reuters dispatch from the 13th)

Rebels Throw 100 Bombs in 20 Minutes, Both Sides Use Aircraft in Combat, Many Civilians Tragically Killed by Bombing

Lisbon. The local radio broadcasting company recently released a message claiming that four planes belonging to the Spanish rebel army departed from Seville last night and flew to Badajoz to drop bombs, dropping a total of 100 bombs of various sizes weighing 30 kilograms each in 20 minutes. (Havas dispatch from the 13th)

Hendaye, France. At the beginning of the Spanish unrest, the government army and the rebel army rarely used air force in combat. Recently, the activities of aircraft on both sides have become increasingly active. This morning, a rebel plane in the north flew to Pasajes to bomb indiscriminately. Many civilians were tragically killed by the bombing. After the government army sent the wounded to the hospital for treatment, it immediately dispatched two planes from the Renteria airfield near San Sebastian to chase the enemy plane. The plane knew that it could not win and fled to the southeast. It is said that it once flew over French territory, but only for a short time. In addition, government planes also flew to San Sebastian and the rebel positions near Renteria this morning to conduct reconnaissance for a long time. It is likely that the government army intends to launch a major offensive, so it is conducting reconnaissance first. Gunshots have been heard in the area since 6:30 this morning, indicating that the war has resumed. The rebel army has been planning to attack Pasajes for a long time, and its planes have been conducting reconnaissance in the villages near the port for days, indicating that its intentions have been planned for more than a day. The government army has probably seen through this strategy, so in order to contain the enemy, it has detained all the prisoners in the military locations that the enemy's artillery can bombard and warned the rebel army to stop firing, otherwise it will execute the prisoners as retaliation. (Havas dispatch from the 13th)

Spain Denies Moving Capital, Where is Rebel Commander-in-Chief Franco? This Raises Doubts

There were rumors that the Spanish government has moved its capital to Valencia, or that it is about to move its capital. The Spanish Embassy in the United Kingdom has recently denied this news on the instructions of the government. (Havas dispatch from the 13th)

Rebel Headquarters in Burgos, The rebel headquarters here today officially raised the fascist flag and the imperial flag. As for the claim that the rebel commander-in-chief General Franco is leading his troops to attack Madrid, it has been circulating for three weeks, but he has not been seen in person. It is doubtful whether he has arrived in southern Spain from Morocco. (National Telegram from the 12th)

Twenty-Five German Planes Arrive at Rebel Headquarters in Spain, Seven Italian Bombers Also Arrive, New York Times Reporter Witnessed

(New York) The New York Times today carried shocking news from a reporter stationed in Seville, Spain, saying that twenty German Junkers heavy bombers and five chase planes, all driven by German military aviators, have flown to the Seville rebel headquarters. This news was sent to Gibraltar by the reporter and then telegraphed to New York. According to the reporter, he personally saw several new German planes, and the pilots were not wearing uniforms. However, the German consul in Seville admitted in private that the personnel were German military aviators. It was also heard from Germans in Seville that the personnel will no longer fly these new planes in the future, but will teach the Spanish how to fly. It was also heard that within a few days, seven Italian Caproni bombers will also arrive in Seville. (Reuters dispatch from the 12th)

(Berlin) The Propaganda Ministry announced today that the claim that twenty-five German planes have arrived in Seville, Spain, is not true and must be inaccurate. According to a senior official of the ministry, the claim by the New York Times correspondent in Seville that the German consulate there admitted that the pilots of the planes were German army aviators is absurd. (Reuters dispatch from the 13th)

Non-Intervention Agreement, Negotiations Among Countries Completed, France's Reservations to Italy Have Not Yet Been Replied

(London) After continuous exchange of opinions among countries, the non-intervention agreement on the Spanish Civil War has been largely completed. The only obstacle that has not yet been resolved is the reservations raised by Italy. The British side hopes that this agreement will be concluded as soon as possible, leaving all minor issues for discussion later. (Reuters dispatch from the 13th)

(Paris) British Ambassador Sir Clerk visited Foreign Minister Delbos today to discuss the situation of the non-intervention agreement negotiations. It is heard that Delbos insisted that this agreement must be concluded quickly. (Havas dispatch from the 12th)

(Rome) Italy has expressed its acceptance of the French draft of the non-intervention agreement and requested the addition of two measures: (1) prohibiting the provision of financial assistance to the two warring parties in Spain, and (2) prohibiting enlistment in the warring parties. According to French sources here, France has not yet replied to Italy's proposals, so it will be difficult to achieve results in the negotiations on the non-intervention agreement today. (Havas dispatch from the 13th)

(Paris) There were rumors that although the French cabinet had decided to adopt a non-intervention policy towards Spain and that all military supplies, including commercial aircraft, were not allowed to be transported to Spain, French aircraft have still been transported to the country in recent days. The government has officially denied this claim. (Havas dispatch from the 12th)

Perpignan, Two truckloads of food donated by the parties of the French Popular Front to the Spanish people have arrived here. (Havas dispatch from the 13th)

Government Forces Besiege Various Cities, Residents Fear Famine, Mountain Militias Increase Construction of Defense Works

Hendaye, France. Government forces are besieging the cities of Toledo, Gijon, and Oviedo today. The residents of the cities are afraid of famine. Although there is a great disparity in the number of government forces and rebel forces, the rebel forces in the cities are still resisting stubbornly. According to a rebel soldier who escaped from Gijon, the situation in the city is very critical. The defenders slaughtered the last horse on Tuesday to fill their stomachs. The rebel general in Oviedo asked the government forces to allow the residents of the city to go out of the city to fetch water for one hour each day. The government forces refused and demanded that the rebel forces surrender unconditionally. Refugees who escaped from Toledo also narrated the tragic situation in the city and the famine among the rebel women and children. (National Telegram from the 12th)

Hendaye, France. A special dispatch from our reporter: Government forces in Guipuzcoa, Spain, have renovated the positions they occupy yesterday. Their positions near Tolosa are still sufficient to control the main roads everywhere. Therefore, although the rebel army has occupied the city, it is not important in the eyes of the government army. In addition, the rebel army attacked the city of Villabona to the south of the city yesterday and was repelled by the government army. The two sides fought fiercely for several hours. The rebel leader once captured an armored car from the government army and killed two soldiers in the car, but in the end, they were still unable to support and retreated. Afterwards, it was heard that the government army executed two wealthy merchants from Tolosa who had been taken hostage in the army as retaliation. Since this morning, the Spanish border has been completely closed. Except for vehicles carrying diplomatic officials, all other vehicles are not allowed to enter the country. According to a person from the Popular Front in the country, the government authorities have taken this measure to prevent the leakage of military secrets and hinder the war. (Havas dispatch from the 13th)

Madrid. The Spanish government announced today that the Asturian miners besieging the city of Oviedo have defeated a column of rebel troops attacking the government forces. At the same time, the government militia that recovered the island of Ibiza in the Balearic Islands was warmly welcomed by the public when it returned to Valencia. The militia will attack Majorca again within days. (Reuters dispatch from the 13th)

Madrid. Regarding the war situation, Interior Minister Pozas stated last night that the militias belonging to the government army in the Somosierra Pass and the Guadarrama Mountains near the capital recently besieged Colonel Aranda's troops who were still trapped in the city of Oviedo. A column of rebel troops attempted to rush to the rescue, but was defeated by the militias of the province. In addition, Colonel Asensio, the former military attaché of the Spanish Embassy in Portugal, told our reporter that the capital Madrid is no longer in danger of being captured by the rebel army, and the rebel army is suffering from food shortages and is exhausted. They are even more disappointed that the reinforcements they were expecting have not arrived. In addition, Prime Minister Quirol stated that President Azana has ordered the dissolution of all monasteries in the country. Furthermore, the Standing Committee of the House of Representatives, which is currently in recess, will meet today to extend the validity period of the various emergency decrees promulgated by the government since the outbreak of the unrest. (Havas dispatch from the 13th)

Madrid. Army Commander-in-Chief General Salaviete recently went to the Somosierra Pass area on the Guadarrama Mountain front north of the capital to inspect military affairs and discussed the war situation north of the capital with General Li Gaimai, commander-in-chief of the northern front. International Commercial Telegraph August 13th, Reuters Special Commercial Report 36

Gold and Silver

London gold price fell one penny today, to one hundred thirty-eight shillings and four pence.

London Silver Market: The silver market remained stable today. Spot and futures prices remained unchanged at 19.5625 pence. Indian buying and selling activities were moderate, with limited trading.

Mountrie Silver Market: Futures opened steady. The November price was 44.75-45.05, one pound lower than yesterday's close.

Exchange Rates

British and American: The London foreign exchange market was quite active today. The pound sterling price was relatively firm. The opening exchange rate between the British pound and the US dollar was $5.025, up 0.03125 from yesterday's close. It continued to rise by 0.01875 one hour later, reaching $5.026875. This price remained unchanged at 1 PM.

Securities

New York Stock Market: The market was slightly cheerful this morning due to positive business reports. Most stocks were active, and prices trended upward. Demand for oil stocks was strong, with the highest price increase. After 11 AM, automobile and railway stocks fell due to speculative pressure, but rebounded at noon. Other stocks also rose slightly compared to yesterday's close. The New York stock market prices are listed below.

Cotton and Wheat

New York Cotton: After the opening, there was some profit-taking in the cotton market. Prices then turned upward due to strong Liverpool telegraphs and good inquiries from fellow traders. Negative weather reports were also a factor in maintaining market confidence. The October futures price at noon was 12.09, up 14 points from yesterday's close.

Liverpool Wheat: The wheat market was firm today. The October futures price at 1 PM rose one penny to seven shillings and five and a quarter pence.

Liverpool Cotton: American cotton futures were firm today. The October futures price at 1 PM was 6.47, up 9 points from yesterday.

Chicago Wheat: The wheat market surged this morning due to firm overseas wheat markets and favorable weather conditions for bulls. Demand from fellow traders further strengthened market prices. The September futures price at noon was 111.875, up 1.375 cents from yesterday's close. The grain market was firm due to news of crop deterioration. The September futures price at noon was 107.5, a net increase of half a cent from yesterday's close.

Rubber

London Rubber: The rubber market was stable. The transaction price for October-December futures at 1 PM was 7.625 pence, the same as yesterday's closing price.

New York Rubber: The rubber market remained quiet and uneventful today. Fellow traders purchased at the opening, and prices rose slightly, but trading was limited. The September futures price at noon was 16.26, up 11 points from yesterday's close. The New York commodity prices are listed below.

Japanese Warship Ataka Arrives in Wuhu Yesterday 37

(Wuhu) The Japanese cruiser Ataka arrived in Wuhu from downstream on the 13th. Officers and sailors went ashore for sightseeing. The departure date from Wuhu is yet to be determined. (Central News Agency, 13th)

Liu Jianxu Arrives in Guiyang Yesterday to Visit Gu 38

(Guiyang) Liu Jianxu arrived in Guiyang by car from the defense area tonight to visit Gu Zhutong and report on defense matters. Gu hosted a banquet for Liu that evening.

Soviet Russia Advances Conscription Age, Germans Believe It Creates a New Situation, Saying It Will Affect the Five-Power European Conference, Japanese Ambassador Ota Returns Home with Reflections 39

(Berlin) Various newspapers here report that because Soviet Russia has reduced the age for conscription to 19 in order to increase the number of army personnel, they all predict that various difficulties will arise when the Locarno Five-Power Conference is held this autumn. People here all believe that this action by the Soviet authorities has created a new situation. Berlin newspapers all believe that the political events before and simultaneous with this Soviet action clearly reveal the aggressive nature of the Soviet Union's military buildup. The Berlin Daily News commented on the current situation, saying that there is no greater danger from the East than there is today. (Reuters, 12th)

(Berlin) According to news from Moscow, the Soviet People's Committee yesterday issued an order advancing the starting age for compulsory military service from 21 to 19. Political figures here were shocked upon hearing the news, believing that the Soviet Union's advance of the military service age would increase its army personnel by 50 percent. It is generally expected that by next year, the country's regular army will have 2 million soldiers, and the reserve army will be 6 million. This is a great danger for Germany. The Berlin Daily News reported that the Soviet Union is sparing no effort in strengthening its military. After the Five-Power Conference is held in the future, Germany's advocacy of a West European non-aggression pact will be even more justified. (Havas, 13th)

Tsuruga: Japanese Ambassador to the Soviet Union, Ota, arrived in Tsuruga at 7 AM on the 13th with his wife and daughter aboard the Siberia Maru from Vladivostok. They then took an international train east. On the train, he told reporters, "I only heard about the detention of personnel from the Japanese Embassy in the Soviet Union while en route. When I was in Moscow, the Soviet side consistently expressed very good intentions. However, not long after I left the Soviet Union, this incident occurred. I do not understand what the real meaning is. Soviet People's Commissar of Defense Voroshilov specifically told me at the farewell banquet when I was returning home that the Soviet Union would absolutely not provoke other countries and asked me to convey this to the Japanese government after returning home. However, it is not known whether these words are true. Although there are frequent rumors of Japan and the Soviet Union going to war, what is the purpose and why must we engage in war? War is not a simple matter. I believe that the Soviet Union's build-up of military equipment is in preparation for invasion by other countries. Ambassadors to the Soviet Union all advocate Japanese-Soviet friendship. Once they return home and hold key positions in the government, they strongly advocate that relations with the Soviet Union are dangerous. Diplomats should not stop until they fully understand the truth when they meet someone. This is probably unavoidable. Therefore, what I say today may all be false, and that is also possible." (Domei, 13th)

Hawaii Islands Expansion of Air Force Plan Airfields Can Accommodate 300 Aircraft 40

Honolulu: The defense of the Hawaiian Islands by the Army and Navy is now impeccable. However, Army and Navy officers still believe that the Air Force needs to be urgently supplemented. The Hickam Airfield, built by the War Department with $18,000,000, is currently under construction. After the completion of Hickam Airfield, along with Luke Airfield and Wheeler Airfield, it can accommodate 200 to 300 aircraft. The Hawaiian Military District also advocates transforming the ancient Kauai Island northwest of Oahu Island and the Hawaiian Island 200 miles away into air base, so that they can become powerful forward observation stations. Currently, the expenses for expanding the Air Force are more than the expenses for the Army and Pearl Harbor Naval Base. The Navy has already tendered for a $10,000,000 floating dock. The $1,500,000 Pearl Harbor dredging project will also be put out to tender. (National News Agency, 12th)

Correction: In yesterday's dispatch from Honolulu on the 11th sent by our agency, this year's expenses should be corrected as follows: the total amount is 20 million US dollars, of which the Navy accounts for approximately 13 million US dollars, and the Army accounts for approximately 7 million US dollars. National News Agency

French Senate Passes Five-Year Air Force Plan, Adding 1,000 Aircraft 41

(Paris) The Senate today discussed the bill on replacing old Air Force aircraft with new ones and daily repairs, and passed it with a unanimous vote. The implementation period of this plan is set at five years, with an annual expenditure of 550,000,000 francs, used to add 1,000 aircraft to replace old ones. During the discussion, Aviation Minister Côte gave a speech, roughly saying, "The total number of aircraft manufactured by France by the end of this year will reach 1,023. However, these aircraft are quickly becoming obsolete. We are now ordering new aircraft to replace them. In short, the government must do its best to ensure that the country has adequate air force equipment to maintain national defense. Maintaining peace also depends on it." (Havas, 12th)

(Paris) The five-year Air Force plan passed by the French Chamber of Deputies, which stipulates an annual expenditure of 550 million francs, was unanimously passed by the Senate today. This plan is based on the principle that the Air Force frontline must have 1,000 aircraft. According to the chairman of the Senate Aviation Committee, Germany now has more than 2,500 aircraft. Aviation Minister Côte also reported to the Senate today that France's air force strength must not lag behind other countries. (Reuters, 12th)

Pacific Institute Meeting Opens in the United States This Week Focus on Japan in Discussions 42

Yosemite National Park, USA: The Sixth Conference of the Pacific Institute will open here this week. At that time, the sudden development of Japan in international trade and economics since its invasion of Manchuria on September 18, 1931, will be discussed in detail. The conference has also asked representatives from China, Japan, the United States, and Russia to clearly state their respective Pacific policies. Members of the institute have also collected extensive materials over the past two years to be presented at the meeting. Regarding the Japan issue, the first aspect is the nature and extent of Japan's external development in recent years. The conference will attempt to determine the scope of Japan's commercial development since 1931 and its monetary value. It will also study the impact of this development on world commerce and the commerce of other Pacific countries. Whether the development in Asia, Africa, and South America is to open up new markets or to seize the markets of other countries, and what is the relationship between the establishment of "Manchukuo" and the commercial development of Japan. That is, whether this development relies solely on the progress of Japan's domestic economic conditions, or whether it is also due to the rich resources of "Manchukuo" that it has been able to achieve this. The conference will also pay special attention to the following points, namely Japan's (1) investment in Manchuria, (2) military actions, and (3) the extent to which government and chaebol subsidies have contributed to this development. Regarding Japan's future economic development policies, the conference will also study two issues. First, whether Japan has formally considered the economic development policies for Manchuria and North China, and second, whether there is a definite plan for Sino-Japanese-"Manchu" economic cooperation. In addition, the conference will also study the relationship between Japan's monetary policy and commercial development, namely how much impact the devaluation of the yen has had, and the reasons for the devaluation, whether it is intended to promote foreign trade, restrict domestic price tightening, or whether it is due to the devaluation of the pound sterling, and whether the yen price can be used as a stable basis. There are also several other issues, listed as follows: (1) What impact does the rise of the world's arms, steel, and chemical industries have on Japan's competition in the world market? (2) What is the relationship between Japan's new investments and new markets in Manchuria and the development of Japan's foreign trade? (3) What impact do the economic crisis and recovery plan in the United States have on Japanese commerce? (4) Is the active competition of Japanese goods in India and the Dutch East Indies caused by the decline of Japanese goods in the Chinese market? (5) How much has the Japanese government's subsidies to the export and transportation industries and other direct assistance since 1931 contributed to commercial development? The conference will finally study the international issues of Japan's national policy, commerce, and monetary system. First, what kind of threats do Pacific countries feel due to Japan's commercial competition? That is, what are the dangers of importing Japanese goods into their own countries and the encroachment of Japanese goods on markets in other countries? Second, what interests are affected by the disputes between Japan and India, the disputes with the Dutch East Indies, the disputes with Canada, and the dissatisfaction of various countries with the closure of the door in Manchuria and North China? Third, how much diplomatic and military pressure will the Japanese government use to obtain tax reductions and other benefits from China that make it difficult for other countries to compete? Fifth, whether Japan can reduce competition in other markets if it reopens the markets in North China and Manchuria? Fifth, what attitude will countries such as Britain and the United States take if Japan further closes the door in North China and Manchuria, and even Central China? (National News Agency, 12th)

American Spy Panic 64

— Translated by Yi Sheng

As the winds of World War II grow tighter by the day, so too do foreign spies along the American coast increase by the day. In the past year alone, it is estimated that European countries spent 50 million US dollars on espionage. In Asia, Japan alone spent 12 million US dollars. They are using various clever methods to steal the secrets of various new and ingenious military weapons.

In recent years, the United States has made many inventions in new military equipment, with the range of mountain guns and mortars exceeding expectations. Semi-automatic rifles can turn every infantryman into a machine gunner. One type of machine gun can fire 150 high-explosive bombs per minute, and a tank driven by seven people can travel at sixty miles per hour. There is also a liquid substance composed of chemicals, gasoline, and explosives, which, if dropped from an airplane, can turn enemy houses into ashes. Although the Army and Navy Departments maintain extreme secrecy regarding the testing of new inventions, foreign spies will do everything possible to find out as soon as they hear about them. Not long ago, the American Martin and Sikorsky aircraft factories successfully manufactured a super aircraft. As soon as this news came out, arms dealers from five countries rushed to the two factories, demanding a preview. Most of these arms dealers are reserve officers who can report directly to their own general staff at any time.

A few months ago, on the docks of New York, just before the Norddeutscher Lloyd ship Europa was about to set sail, a person in civilian clothes, carrying a violin case, strode onto the gangplank, intending to board the ship. At this moment, a plainclothes detective stepped forward, detained him, and found in the violin case a large number of military maps, secret documents, weapons blueprints, the latest aircraft designs, and blueprints for foldable machine guns used in newly invented fighter planes. It turned out that the man wanted to hand the violin case to a steward on the ship, who would then take it to a certain country in Europe. This act of espionage was only dealt with by deportation, because American laws against espionage are very lenient.

Not long ago, a foreign spy came to the United States and became friends with a reserve officer. The officer was proficient in chemistry and had worked in government agencies. The spy bribed him with 25,000 US dollars to steal a copy of the formula for the chemicals used in American army gas masks. The officer, in urgent need of money, went to a certain deputy in the chemistry lab and promised him a reward of 10,000 US dollars. Unexpectedly, the deputy informed the director of this matter. As a result, the officer only received the punishment of dismissal.

Also, a certain important American official was traveling home by train from Washington, D.C. The briefcase he was carrying contained various designs related to national defense. During the journey, two strangers came to talk to him, and after getting off the train, they followed him. Not long after, he discovered that the desk in his office had been pried open. It turned out that someone had secretly given his servant 500 dollars to steal the important documents.

Waste paper from government agencies is often bought by people from the janitors for large sums of money. The US Patent Office is also a place frequented by spies. They often carry large sums of money to visit inventors and seek technical secrets. The inventor of the American new-style tank, Christie, once rejected their request, and they replied, "You'd better sell it, otherwise, we'll steal it anyway."

In February of this year, the US Army Department, in order to be cautious about military secrets, issued very strict instructions. Anyone who leaks any military secrets to anyone will be sentenced to two years in prison. Anyone who sells or gives military secrets to foreigners will be sentenced to twenty years in prison.

Not long ago, a foreign scientist, while slowly touring a certain arsenal, suddenly lifted his coat and used a small camera attached to his suspenders to photograph a certain important component. This small camera looked like a button on the suspenders. Fortunately, it was immediately discovered by the factory personnel.

The US Navy seems to be threatened by a fleet of spy ships. This sounds strange. However, the American naval and army officers firmly believe it, because there is a fleet diagram drawn by government surveyors as evidence. The diagram depicts a large fishing boat with a continuous cruising range of eight thousand miles, equipped with powerful searchlights and wireless radios. There are now as many as 250 of these ships along the American Pacific coast. They usually travel back and forth under the guise of fishing, and in wartime, the fish holds and bait storage rooms inside the ships can be immediately converted into mines and torpedo tubes. Moreover, most of the crew members are naval reservists who can start attacking American warships one hour after the two countries go to war. Recently, these disguised warships have been closely following the American fleet at all times, especially when American warships are conducting target practice.

Because the laws are too lenient, it is very difficult to crack down on spies. A famous government secret agent once said, "Catching kidnappers is easier than catching spies."

Page 11

Japanese Merchants Acquire Huaxin Yarn Factory for 1.2 Million Yuan; Buyer is Kanegafuchi Spinning Company 65

Tianjin Dispatch: The Huaxin Yarn Factory has been sold to the Japanese. A preliminary agreement was signed on the evening of the 9th. The buyer is the Japanese Kanegafuchi Spinning Company. The signing took place at the residence of Liu Junqing, a director of Huaxin Yarn Factory. The Japanese representative was Kurachi, a director of Kanegafuchi Spinning Company, and the Huaxin representative was Liu Junqing. Xu Jishang was also present, and the lawyer Lin Xinggui acted as a witness. The selling price is 1.2 million yuan. The preliminary agreement consists of five items: (1) A deposit of 100,000 yuan will be paid on the signing date; (2) The remaining 1.1 million yuan will be paid in full upon taking over the factory; (3) The existing stock of cotton yarn, etc., will be paid for in cash by the new owner at a discounted price; (4) All factory employees will be retained for three months, and all workers will be retained for six months; (5) This agreement is effective from the date of signing. On the 11th, Kurachi, accompanied by several Japanese technicians, inspected the Huaxin Yarn Factory to examine the machinery, and it was decided that the takeover would be completed within twenty days. On September 1st, work will be suspended for five days to complete the takeover procedures, clean up the interior, and dismiss workers, etc. It is agreed by both parties that all relevant regulations will comply with the factory laws of our Ministry of Industry. After the new owner takes over, the factory name will be changed to Gongda No. 7 Factory. Repairs to the machinery, as well as the addition of new machines and looms, will have to wait until next year. For the time being, the status quo will be maintained, and work will resume on September 6th. The factory has a total of 32,000 old and new yarn spindles, with 25,000 currently in operation, and 1,400 workers. The Tangshan, Qingdao, and Weihui factories are unrelated to this and operate independently. The name "Gongda No. 7 Factory" is based on the order in which Kanegafuchi Spinning Company's yarn factories are arranged in its own country. The Tianjin Yuyuan Yarn Factory was also acquired by Kanegafuchi Spinning Company and renamed Gongda No. 6 Factory. Therefore, in Tianjin alone, Kanegafuchi Spinning Company now has two factories, with a total of 106,000 yarn spindles (74,000 in Yuyuan). Recently, Kurachi came to North China to investigate and is planning to build a yarn factory in Shihe. If this is realized, then the company's yarn industry power will be enough to control the overall situation in North China.

Huaxin's sale this time is partly blamed on the difference of opinion among the directors, with many holding dissenting views and advocating for selling off the factory to avoid further losses, and partly blamed on the Tianjin industrial and financial circles and the government sitting idly by without providing assistance. The banking syndicate, having already invested in establishing the Chengfu Trust Company to manage the Beiyang and Hengyuan yarn factories, with a total investment of more than 1.4 million yuan, seems to have no intention of investing further substantial funds in operating Huaxin. The Social Affairs Bureau, which is related to the yarn factory business, has recently undergone frequent personnel changes, with the director changing repeatedly, and almost no one paying attention to this matter. Although a special commissioner was dispatched to investigate, there was no effective way to provide relief. A week ago, Huaxin proposed a self-rescue plan, earnestly requesting government officials to negotiate with the banking community to borrow 1.5 million yuan, with 1 million yuan to be used to repay foreign debts and shareholder deposits, and 500,000 yuan to be used to purchase new machines to compete with the Japanese. However, the Social Affairs Bureau did not pay attention to it, and the banking community was unwilling to accept the factory's request. Under the delay, the Japanese side actively proceeded. Initially, the Japanese Toyo Spinning Company and Kanegafuchi Spinning Company offered equal prices, and the competition was fierce. They sought direct intervention from the Japanese Consul-General in Tianjin. The Japanese Consul-General found it difficult to mediate and transferred the matter to the military for arbitration. The military, because Toyo Spinning Company had already built a large-scale Yufeng branch factory in Tianjin, in order to ensure a balanced business power between the two entities in the future and avoid an excessively skewed situation, ruled that Kanegafuchi Spinning Company should acquire the factory. After receiving the promise, the company successfully negotiated the deal within a few days. From now on, Huaxin is no longer ours. (11th)

Situation After the Puppet Troops Disturbed Eastern Suiyuan; A Certain Party's Supervising Team Arrives in Zhangbei; It is Rumored that Fu Zuoyi is Doing His Utmost to Preserve the Territory 66

Beijing Dispatch: The joint intrusion into Eastern Suiyuan by bandits and puppet troops from Chahar has aroused attention and concern from all parties. Although the tense situation in that area has not diminished slightly since the 4th of this month, there have been no significant changes in the situation. Whether this issue will escalate completely depends on a certain party that is in control. According to a certain person familiar with the situation in Mongolia, it is an undeniable fact that a certain party is plotting to control Mongolia, and this has been going on for a long time. However, the current path has not been decided, and the implementation has not been sufficiently prepared. Therefore, in the very short term, it is expected that there will be no direct military action to seize Eastern Suiyuan. Most of those who intruded into Eastern Suiyuan this time were bandits and puppet troops. The bandits were from Wang Daoyi's gang and scattered bandits newly recruited from Hebei Province. The puppet troops were from Li Shouxin's rebel troops and the security forces of Zhuosh Hai's unit in Inner Mongolia. Although the number reached 10,000, they were mostly a motley crowd. After being defeated in this intrusion, they are now reorganizing. The troops that a certain party recently sent to Zhangbei totaled two regiments, which together with the Chinese army, amounted to about two regiments. Their purpose is to supervise the battle, and their nature is like that of a supervising team. With this small number of troops, it is unlikely that they will dare to attack. Moreover, there are not many troops in Rehe Province other than the militia. From this, it can be seen that a certain party is still mainly instigating bandits to intrude. If they achieve their goal, they can sit back and enjoy the success; otherwise, they may temporarily adopt a wait-and-see attitude.

De Wang himself is in a very difficult situation. He is still in Jiabu Temple. The rumor that he has gone to Bailing Temple to handle the closing of the Mongolian Political Council is not true, and it is also impossible. De Wang once told a certain party, "You can do whatever you want; I don't want to advocate anything." From this, we can see De Wang's intention. Li Shouxin, who is now in Shangdu, also said, "I once commanded the Volunteer Army. What was the task I was responsible for at that time? How can I be willing to be a traitor now? I personally am not a problem, but I must plan for the resettlement of my subordinates. Therefore, the current situation has arisen. In the future, I will definitely seek a way to ensure both aspects and protect my past reputation."

The Suiyuan authorities foresaw the bandit's invasion four months ago. At that time, Pu Province was carrying out a large-scale purge of the remaining communists in the territory. Chairman Fu Zuoyi of Suiyuan was also in Shanxi. Regarding this matter, Fu had discussed everything with Yan Xishan and decided to do his utmost to preserve the territory. After Mr. Fu returned to Suiyuan, he began to make arrangements. The fortifications along the Ping-Sui line have now been completed. Mr. Fu's current tour is to inspect everything. (12th)

Assassination Case in Zhangzhou: Weng Cixing Assassinated After Reforming; Seventeen Bullets Hit, Died on the Spot; Two Assassins Both Escaped 67

Xiamen Dispatch: An assassination case occurred in Zhangzhou at 8:15 p.m. on the 9th, creating a tense situation. The deceased was Weng Cixing, the former commander of the pseudo "Fujian Fourth Detachment of the Chinese Revolutionary Alliance Army," who had reformed not long ago. The two assassins both escaped. According to investigations, Weng was a well-known local communist in Zhangzhou and Xiamen during the era when Zhang Zhen, the commander of the 49th Division, was stationed in Zhangzhou before the 20th year of the Republic. During the Fujian Incident, he served as a leading figure in the pseudo People's Government Farmers' Association. After the Fujian Incident was quelled, Weng fled to Hong Kong and Shanghai, and later joined Chen Mingshu's pseudo "Chinese National Revolutionary Datong Alliance." Chen appointed him to secretly organize the "Heng Society" in Xiamen and Gulangyu, recruiting bandits and hooligans, and also served as the commander of the pseudo Alliance Army. In the early summer of this year, he was arrested in Xiamen and sent to the Zhangzhou Pacification Commissioner's Office. Later, he was allowed to reform. Weng issued a declaration, exposing Chen Mingshu and Li Jishen's conspiracy to form a pseudo alliance. After reforming, he served as an intelligence officer in the Commissioner's Office. On the evening of the 9th, at around 8 p.m., Weng left his home at No. 24 Luan'an South Road, and someone immediately followed him. When he reached the front of No. 7 Luan'an West Road, an assassin shot Weng with a Mauser pistol from a distance of three or four steps behind. Weng was hit by two bullets and fell to the ground. The assassin then repeatedly shot Weng's chest and abdomen more than ten times. Another assassin caught up and fired several shots with a Browning pistol. The gunshots were like a string of firecrackers. Stray bullets slightly injured two passers-by. The scene was the bustling central market of Zhangzhou. Pedestrians were numerous, and they were shocked and fled when they heard the incident. Merchants did not know what had happened and closed their doors. Before long, the effect spread to the entire city. The assassins escaped in the confusion. When the military police rushed to the scene, Weng was barely breathing and soon died. His right hand was still gripping the handle of the Browning pistol he was carrying at his left waist, as if he wanted to draw his gun to resist but was unable to do so. An examination of his body revealed that he had been hit by a total of seventeen bullets, and his entire body was covered in blood. The city defense command immediately announced martial law, surrounded and searched the vicinity, but found nothing. At around 1 a.m., martial law was further tightened, and household registrations were checked. The investigation was completed at 4 or 5 a.m. on the 10th. Sentries were posted on all major roads in the southeast, northwest, and northeast suburbs to prevent the assassins from escaping. After dawn, the sentries saw a suspicious person inside the West Gate Lake, ordered him to stop, and the person immediately pulled out a Mauser pistol to resist and was shot dead on the spot. It was found that he was Ma Hao, a member of Gao Weinan's bandit gang who had already been sentenced. Nothing else was found. That night, the city defense department banned the publication of news. The ban was lifted the next day. The reason for Weng's assassination is unclear. (August 13th)

Ancient Trees in Southern Anhui Abusively Felled by Mountain People; Jing-Qu Railway Plans to Purchase Sleepers Locally at a Given Price; Mountain People, Thinking They Would Be Requisitioned Without Payment, Destroyed the Trees in Advance 68

Wuhu Dispatch: Ninguo, Jingxian, Jingde, Langxi, and Guangde counties in southern Anhui are mostly mountainous and rich in natural forests. A large amount of pine timber and charcoal is exported every year. Among them, chestnut and elm are all useful materials. The Anhui Provincial Government, in line with the purpose of promoting forestry, specifically consulted with the Ministry of Railways and planned to use chestnut and elm produced in the above counties for sleeper materials for the Jing-Qu Railway, which is under construction and passes through Anhui Province. The selling price is not only cheaper than imported products, but there is also no transportation hassle. The Ministry of Railways agreed to this. After both parties finalized the agreement, the Anhui Construction Bureau summoned timber merchants from the above-mentioned areas to Wuhu for talks, and agreed on a number of payment and contract methods. Unexpectedly, most mountain owners, for some reason, developed a huge misunderstanding, fearing that timber merchants would arbitrarily requisition timber in the future without paying a price. They abused and felled ancient trees that had been growing for many years, causing a large number of useful and good materials to be destroyed and turned into firewood. Timber merchants Chen Daofu and Shi Zhenqi, etc., were greatly alarmed by this news. The earthworks for the railway have already started, and the track is being laid in sections, and the time is near. Not only will this delay the railway work, but the provincial government's credibility with the Ministry of Railways is also greatly affected. Timber merchants contract for work with fair prices, and it is not using government officials to arbitrarily requisition. It is really no different than commercial trade. If not promptly and strictly stopped, the damage is unimaginable. A joint petition was submitted to the Xuancheng Ninth Administrative District Commissioner's Office to investigate and prohibit the indiscriminate felling of ancient trees by mountain owners. After receiving the petition, the Commissioner's Office immediately sent a telegram to various places, ordering them to persuade and admonish the mountain owners. (12th)

Kunshan: County Court Site Determined 69

The Ministry of Judicial Administration previously informed the Jiangsu Provincial Government that courts should be established uniformly in all counties within three years. Later, the Provincial Government believed that this plan had many obstacles and that its economic strength was insufficient, so it specifically informed the Ministry that it planned to establish courts in the province separately within six years. The Ministry then replied in agreement and established the courts in phases. It is now learned that after receiving the order, the County Government is actively preparing. County Magistrate Peng and Trial Officer Cao also surveyed a Wang family house on Xitang Street in the city to be the site of the County Court and reported it to the High Court for filing. Yang Yuande, a resident of Pingting Town in the Second District of the county, is over fifty years old, but suffers from a mental illness. He often goes out and causes trouble. Although he has been treated once, it has not been eradicated. Recently, Yang's old illness relapsed. At about 4 p.m. on the 12th, he suddenly broke into the Second District Office of the town and caused trouble. When the town officials saw this, they immediately ordered the yamen runner to tell his mother, Yang Hu, to come and dissuade him. Not only did he refuse to listen, but he took scissors and chased and beat his mother, causing deep wounds to Mrs. Hu's neck and chest and abdomen. Her ribs were broken, and she fell to the ground and died on the spot. When the townspeople saw that Yang had caused a major disaster, they immediately reported it to the competent public security substation. Inspector Zhang ordered Chief Policeman Hu Bin and Special Police Zhang Mingtang to carry live ammunition rifles and rush to the scene to suppress him. When Yang saw that the police had arrived, he resisted and attempted to commit violence. Special Officer Wang Mingtang immediately raised his gun and fired at Yang Yuande, hitting him in the buttocks. He collapsed due to excessive blood loss and died before he could be treated. The substation immediately sent a telegram to the County Government, which dispatched Trial Officer Cao to lead officials to the scene to inspect the body and provide coffins. Special Police Officer Wang Mingtang was sent to the County Government for interrogation.

Civil Servants and Citizens Swear an Oath 70

The county's civil servants, self-governing personnel, and citizens' oath ceremony was held at 2 p.m. on the 13th in the County Government's auditorium. More than 600 people participated. Chairman Zhang Yi of the First District led the reading of the oath. Then, County Magistrate Peng Baichuan delivered a speech and the photography ceremony was completed.

Guangdong Province's Issue of Changing to the Silver Dollar System; The Exchange Rate Between Silver Dollars and Small Silver Coins is Under Discussion; Business Community Believes the Exchange Rate Should Not Exceed Three 71

Guangzhou Dispatch: The Guangdong Provincial Government is actively preparing for the implementation of the silver dollar system. Finance Director Song Ziliang and Ju Zuyi took a plane from Guangdong to Lushan on the 11th specifically for the reform, to ask Minister Kong for instructions on everything. In the future, there will be no problem with the Bank of Communications and the Central Bank issuing silver dollar notes in Guangdong. However, the standard for the exchange rate between the silver dollar and Guangdong silver certificates has not yet been determined, and experts have been enthusiastically discussing this point in recent days. Some advocate adding 1.44 to the silver certificate exchange rate with silver dollars, that is, every 100 yuan of silver dollars exchanges for 144 yuan of Guangdong silver certificates. Some advocate adding 1.25, that is, 100 yuan of silver dollars exchanges for 125 yuan of Guangdong silver certificates. The arguments are diverse, each with its own reasons. Therefore, the Finance Authorities have not yet stipulated the exchange rate between silver dollars and silver certificates. Recently, the Guangdong business community has also proposed opinions on setting the exchange rate. According to the Silver Industry Association, the ratio of silver dollars to silver certificates should be no more than three, because in the past, the collection of national taxes in Guangdong Province was paid with silver certificates plus 25% for water. If calculated with a ratio of three, the difference is minimal. If the difference in the exchange rate is too large (some advocate adding six), Guangdong people will bear heavy taxes and prices will increase accordingly. Therefore, it is advocated that the rate should not be too disparate, so as not to hinder the implementation of the currency unification. As for the Guangzhou General Chamber of Commerce, it also listed its opinions on the exchange rate between silver dollars and Guangdong certificates yesterday and telegraphed Minister Kong to approve the implementation. The telegraph stated as follows: "The reason for Guangdong Province's conversion to the silver dollar system is to seek currency unification. However, this matter is closely related to the interests of the people of Guangdong. Our association has collected the opinions of many merchants. The highest rate for exchanging small silver coins for silver dollars cannot exceed three. The reasons are as follows: (1) The exchange rate for changing to silver dollars should be based on the reserve fund, but the government is still continuing to purchase silver, so the amount of the reserve fund cannot be precisely calculated. As far as the current situation is concerned, in addition to the 100 million yuan of silver already collected, the assets of other provincial and municipal banks and the value of the construction of sugar factories, yarn factories, and earthworks, together with public bonds and borrowings, are estimated to be more than 200 million yuan. In the future, when more silver is collected, Guangdong Province's reserve fund will be even greater. (2) Guangdong Province's small silver certificates have always been exchanged for silver at current rates. Although there was a move to purchase silver at a rate of two last year, the people did not actually benefit from it. All of the silver owned by the people of Guangdong is deposited and transacted at the silver certificate number and exchanged back to legal currency, which is more than several times the number purchased by the government. It can be seen that the general public has not benefited from the two-for-one exchange. (3) For more than 20 years, the highest amount of silver dollars received in national taxes in Guangdong Province has been calculated at a rate of three over silver certificates, that is, the ordinary market price is also between two and three. The abnormal mutation cannot be used as a basis for argument. Furthermore, the merchants and people of Guangdong Province have raised huge amounts of money to help the revolutionary army over the years and have made huge sacrifices. Now that the overall situation is the same and the currency system has changed, the people of Guangdong are afraid that the silver dollar ratio will be set too high, and they are all at a loss. We respectfully telegraph to your office for review and approval, requesting that the Guangdong Finance Office order that the highest silver dollar ratio for small silver coins must not exceed three, in order to appease public opinion, and request a telegraphic instruction to comply. Sincerely, Guangzhou General Chamber of Commerce." (August 11th)

Suzhou: Agricultural Bank Staff Embezzlement Case 72

Wang Cainan (Zhengrong), the former director of the teller department of the Suzhou Farmers Bank, absconded with 150,000 yuan last year. Although the matter has been reported to the authorities for investigation, there has been no news to this day. Liu Zhaoxiang, the president of the bank, suspected that Shi Zongding, the teller department staff member who had been dismissed from the bank, was complicit in the matter and filed a complaint with the local court, accusing Shi Zongding of embezzlement. The local court held a hearing on the morning of the 10th. Both the plaintiff and the defendant were summoned to the court and questioned by Judge Fang Qinghuan. Shi Zongding was ordered to pay a written bail of 1,000 yuan and released, pending investigation and further interrogation.

The County Public Security Bureau recently discovered that a large number of fake five-yuan and one-yuan banknotes have been found on the market, disrupting the financial system. Paving the Suzhou-Wuxi Road Surface 74

Changzhou, Luoyang Town Robbery and Assault 76

Yangzhou, Water Conservancy Association Surveying Riverbank Collapse 77

The riverbank along the Jiangbei area has been collapsing year by year, resulting in significant losses. Previously, local figures in Yangzhou organized a Riverbank Protection Association to appeal for action. Later, during the National Water Conservancy Conference in Beijing, Mr. Han Zhishi, a respected elder from Taixian, specifically submitted a proposal to construct a water dam to protect against the collapse. The proposal was unanimously approved. It is now learned that the National Economic Council has instructed the Yangtze River Water Conservancy Association and the Hydraulic Engineering Testing Institute to conduct surveys and tests in accordance with the resolution. It is also learned that Mr. Han has informed the Riverbank Protection Association to promptly and accurately compile statistics on the annual collapse measurements and locations, to serve as reference materials for the model construction.

Water District Gun Loss Case Cracked 78

Nine box-type guns, four handguns, and 2,700 bullets were stolen while Shen Jinghua was the former district chief of the Fourth District of the Guazhou Water Police. For many days, the stolen items were not recovered. Recently, Zhu Xinke, the head of the district's detective team, was instructed to strictly investigate the case. He obtained information from informants and captured Sun Desheng and a Mr. Fan outside the South Gate of Zhenjiang, recovering a handgun and 50 bullets. Fan confessed that he currently works as a clerk in the First Branch Bureau of the provincial capital. The stolen guns and bullets from the district office were entirely the work of Cao Jinyuan, a sergeant in the former district office's special task force, who entrusted Li Xingsheng, who was stationed in the countryside outside the South Gate, to sell them. Based on the confession, Captain Zhu led detectives such as Miao Tongfu and arrested Li in Mingguang County, Anhui. They continued to search the home of Liu Zhaolin in Jiulipu, Second District of Jiangdu, recovering 1,318 bullets. Liu was a cook in the former district office. Liu was taken back for questioning. It was later learned that Cao Jinyuan, the prime suspect in the case, had fled and was hiding in Daluzhen Town outside Zhenjiang City. He was reported to the security team and tax police for carrying a handgun in the bathhouse. When the tax police arrived to arrest him, Cao opened fire and was killed on the spot. Only one accomplice, Chen Yongde, a box-type gun and dozens of bullets were captured. He has been taken back by the tax police for questioning. Captain Zhu, after hearing the news, has sent a letter to the tax police team to bring Chen and the guns and bullets back for further investigation.

Taicang, Madman Kills Mother, Shot Dead 79

Yang Yuande, a resident of Beijie, Penglai Town, First District of the county, was in his thirties and had a history of mental illness. Yesterday afternoon, he had a severe episode and beat his mother violently. His mother, terrified by the sight, fled to a nearby barbershop. Yang followed her in, seized a razor, and stabbed his mother in the chest and abdomen. She was instantly covered in blood and flesh and died on the spot. Neighbors reported the incident to the Kunshan Public Security Bureau's branch office, which dispatched police to arrest him. Yang, with extraordinary strength, wielded the knife wildly, making it impossible to approach him. They opened fire, shooting him dead. Bullets flew everywhere, causing panic among the residents of the town. The Qiantang River Bridge project was slightly affected by the Qiantang River's current last month, but the water level soon dropped, and work has been accelerated. Caisson No. 5, which was washed to near Nanxing Bridge by the flood, has now been towed to Pier No. 10 for construction. Pier No. 1 on the north bank was completed earlier last month. The Pier No. 1 project is expected to be completed by the end of August. The piling work has been completed in eight locations. All 16 steel beams for the bridge, each 220 meters long and weighing approximately 260 tons, have arrived and are scheduled to be erected by the end of September and completed by the end of June next year.

Taizhou, Wenling Drought Established 80

Since the early rice harvest in Wenling County, there has been no rain, and a drought has been established. The water in the city streams has dried up, and the springs and wells have run dry, affecting drinking water. Most of the crops in the surrounding villages have withered, sweet potato vines have dried up, and taro leaves have withered. The weather has been hot for days, with no sign of rain. If this continues for another ten days, the autumn harvest will be hopeless. Rice merchants in various towns and cities are taking the opportunity to raise rice prices, and laborers are crying out in despair.

Jiaxing, Police Officer Shoots and Kills Villager 81

Li Liangsheng (also known as Li Yuanguan), a villager from the second household of the second Jia of the fourth Bao in Fengzuiqiao Town, Jiaxing, was reported to the police for suspected involvement in selling earth. On the morning of the 12th, Zhang, the director of the Fengqiao Public Security Bureau, led all the police officers to surround Li's front and back doors and begin the search. Li Liangsheng, unaware of the situation, tried to escape when he left the house. He was shot by the guarding police officer, who hit his lower back, a vital area. Li fell to the ground and died on the spot. The police officers, seeing that they had caused a disaster, hurried back to the bureau. Subsequently, the deceased's younger brother reported the incident to the town government, and the town chief, Feng Xiangbo, reported it to the Jiaxing District Court. The court sent officials to investigate on the 13th and summoned the police officer who fired the shot to begin an investigation. Tang Jinmao, a traveler at the Yadong Hotel in Jiaxing, (from Jintan, currently a sericulture instructor in Danyang County), attempted suicide by drinking mercury chloride on the night of August 3rd and left five letters. After the discovery, he was sent to the Gospel Hospital for treatment. After rescue efforts, there was no significant change in his condition. However, from the 9th, the poison had entered his internal organs, and he vomited and had diarrhea, both of which were fresh blood. He even became manic and attacked anyone he saw. He died on the 11th due to ineffective treatment. The Public Security Bureau was immediately notified and reported the matter to the District Court. On the 12th, the court sent officials to investigate. Gu Jinghua, the head of the Daohua Seed Breeding Farm, arranged for the coffin and burial and notified his family to come to He to collect the coffin for burial.

Citizen Registration Oath Taking in the City 84

Various government agencies will hold the oath-taking ceremony today; professional associations will swear in on the 16th; The French Consul General instructs the police department to assist.

The citizen registration oath-taking ceremony in the city has been prepared by the National Assembly Election Office for several days and is scheduled to be held in sequence starting today. In the Second Special District, the French Consul has instructed the police department to assist the sub-offices in handling the matter. The Boy Scouts, due to the short timeframe, were notified by the National Assembly Election Office to extend their service. The details are as follows:

Oath-taking Ceremony for Party and Government Agencies Today

Today (14th), the agencies holding the citizen registration oath-taking ceremony are: The various agencies in the city center district, at 9:00 AM in the City Hall auditorium; The City Public Security Bureau, at 9:00 AM at its location on Penglai Road; The City Party Headquarters and various district party headquarters, at 1:00 PM at the City Party Headquarters; The National Assembly Election Office, at 1:00 PM at the office; The various agencies in Fenglinqiao, at 4:00 PM in the Foreign Affairs Building. The Office has appointed the chairman and oath administrators for each location. They will lead the staff, carrying citizen registration forms and oaths, to preside over the ceremony. The agencies have been notified to convene for the event. Tomorrow (15th), the oath-taking ceremony for the staff of the various district party headquarters and the members of the various district branches will be held at 9:00 AM at the respective district party headquarters.

Scheduled Oath-taking Ceremony for Professional Associations

The National Assembly Election Office issued Notice No. 5 yesterday, stating, "It is hereby stipulated that the date and location for the staff of various professional associations in this city to complete citizen oath-taking registration are as follows: Farmers' Association and Fishermen's Association, date: August 16th, 9:00 AM, location: City Farmers' Association; Labor Union, date: August 16th, 9:00 AM, location: Meijia Lane City General Labor Union; Chamber of Commerce, date: August 16th, 9:00 AM, location: City Chamber of Commerce. The directors, councilors, executive and supervisory committee members, and alternate executive and supervisory committee members of each of the aforementioned organizations, as well as the directors, councilors, executive and supervisory committee members, and alternate executive and supervisory committee members of the various district farmers' associations, industry labor unions, and trade associations under their jurisdiction, shall proceed to the aforementioned date and location to complete citizen registration and oath-taking. This matter concerns citizenship qualifications; do not neglect it. This is hereby published for public notice."

Oath Wording Prescribed by the National Government

The citizen registration forms and oath forms have been printed in large quantities by the office. The oath is as follows: "Oath: ×××, with sincerity and intention, solemnly swear before the public that from this day forward, I will abandon the old and embrace the new, stand as a citizen, devote my loyalty and effort to uphold the Republic of China, implement the Three Principles of the People, adopt the Five-Power Constitution, strive to achieve political clarity and people's happiness, establish a solid foundation for the nation, and maintain world peace. This I swear, the Republic of China, ×× year, ×× month, ×× day (signed)." "Note: The year, month, and day should be filled with the date of the oath; the oath should be returned to the public office after the oath is taken."

Police Assistance in the Second Special District

City Party Headquarters Issues Notice to Citizens for Citizen Registration and Oath-taking Yesterday 85

The National News Agency reported that the City Party Headquarters issued a notice to citizens yesterday regarding citizen registration and citizen oath-taking. The original text is as follows: "Dear compatriots, the National Assembly will be held on November 12th of this year. This is an excellent opportunity for us to participate in national politics. However, to participate in national politics and exercise our rights to elect, recall, initiate, and referendum, we must first obtain citizenship. How can we obtain citizenship? Simply put, anyone over the age of twenty, regardless of gender, who has not committed a crime or has a mental illness can register with the citizen registration office. After completing the citizen oath-taking procedure, they obtain citizenship and have citizen rights. Citizen registration and citizen oath-taking have now begun in this city. We hope that the general public will understand the following points: First, the significance of holding this citizen registration and citizen oath-taking is profound. Those who register and take the oath obtain citizenship and become good citizens who accept the Three Principles of the People, and they can participate in the election of this year's National Assembly. Therefore, it can also be said that this is a prerequisite for the people to participate in national politics. Second, promoting local autonomy is the foundation for realizing the principle of people's rights. If local autonomy is successfully promoted, the people will be able to manage local affairs, and then they will be able to participate in national affairs, develop true people's rights, and permanently establish the foundation of the Republic of China. To achieve this goal, everyone must fulfill citizen registration and citizen oath-taking. At the same time, we hope that everyone will actively fulfill citizen registration and citizen oath-taking. (Slogans) Fulfilling citizen registration and citizen oath-taking is the only way to obtain citizenship; With citizenship, the people have the right to participate in politics; Giving up citizenship is not a virtue of the people; Respecting citizenship is respecting one's own personality; Quickly and actively fulfill citizen registration and citizen oath-taking."

City Chamber of Commerce Requests Temporary Suspension of Inspection of Artificial Silk Piece Goods, Silk Weaving Products from Various Provinces Will Be Unable to Be Transported and Sold 86

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance, stating, "Respectful report to the Honorable Customs Administration of the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, regarding the domestic artificial silk woven products sold by silk merchants in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, which are purchased in small quantities from local weaving households, assembled into whole units, and then sold in batches to merchants from various provinces. The weaving households purchase silk in small quantities from local firms, and the original artificial silk importers have already resold it six, seven, or even ten times. There is no way to obtain tax receipts or exchange them for licenses. Representatives of the industry, such as Luo Qinghua, have already explained this in detail to Section Chief Wu of your administration during their petition, and we believe they were understood. We request that the articles of the inspection and clearance of artificial silk piece goods be revised. Before the regulations are revised, we request a temporary suspension of implementation. Otherwise, starting tomorrow, silk woven products from various provinces will be unable to be transported and sold, and weaving households and silk merchants will be unable to make a living. We beg for a speedy review and response by telegram. The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce respectfully submits."
