Silver Import Surplus 88

The government's purpose in reforming the currency system is to: Unify issuance, Centralize reserves, Preserve silver, Revitalize industry. Its aim is to prevent our country's currency from being affected by the fluctuations of the world bank and to achieve independence in order to promote the revival of the national economy. Since the implementation of the new monetary policy, foreign exchange has remained stable, and silver exports were highest in December of last year, with an export surplus of 66,608 yuan. However, by January of this year, the export surplus decreased to 15,416,432 yuan. Since then, it has changed to an import surplus. For example, in April, the import surplus was 92,349 yuan, which is a very small amount, but it can be said that the government's purpose of preserving silver has been fully achieved.

Bank Deposits in This City Exceed 600 Million Yuan 89

The East China News Agency reported that the deposits in more than 40 banks in this city for the first half of this year, according to the finalized accounts published, amount to 21, with no reports from the rest. In total, the more than 40 banks have more than 600 million yuan in current and fixed deposits. According to the Savings Bank Law, 120 million yuan of this amount must be lent to rural areas. However, due to current circumstances, the amount of loans to rural areas in the city is only 20 to 30 million yuan, which is far from the regulation. Now that the Rural Development Bureau is about to be established, the stagnant funds in the banking sector have slightly improved, but the proportion is only 1% of the deposits. Therefore, economic circles hope that the government and the financial sector will cooperate and stipulate that a few more percentage points be set aside for industrial loans. If necessary, a "Industrial Capital Bureau" similar to the Rural Bureau should be established to jointly invest.

China Yangtze River Pilotage Recommends Representatives to Petition in Beijing Again, Thoroughly Recovering Water Rights and Transferring Management to the Ministry of Communications 92

China's Yangtze River pilotage has been appealing for the recovery of water rights, the promulgation of pilotage laws, and the transfer of management to the Ministry of Communications. The Central People's Training Department sent personnel to investigate in April of this year, and in early June, they told the petitioning representatives that they would invite relevant ministries and commissions to discuss the matter. The petitioning representatives listened and returned. Now that two months have passed, the entire body of pilots has resolved to recommend Feng Fucheng, the chairman of the Pilotage Association, as a representative to petition in Beijing. He departed last night. The China Seafarers' Party, due to its responsibilities, has also sent Hu Qi, the director of the worker training department, to Beijing to forward everything to the Central Government. Recovering water rights is of great importance to the livelihood of all national pilots and to national defense and navigation. Pilot Representative Feng Fucheng will petition the Central Party Headquarters, the Legislative Yuan, the Executive Yuan, and various relevant departments in Beijing this time. It is hoped that this petition will result in practical measures to comfort the hopes of the pilots nationwide.

Beijing Municipal Central Trust Bureau Loan Contract Signed and Funds Released, Various Projects Underway, Expected to Be Completed in One Year 93

The Nanjing Municipal Government borrowed 1.7 million yuan from the Central Trust Bureau to expand the capital's water supply facilities and drainage projects. Mayor Ma Chaojun and Bureau Director Ye Zhuotang finalized the agreement in Shanghai at the end of last month, stipulating a five-year term with a weekly interest rate of 8%, starting the repayment of principal and interest from July of the second year. The capital's water supply plant's entire property and the city's special construction bonds with a face value of 600,000 yuan were used as collateral. A reporter from the New Voice News Agency interviewed Bureau Deputy Director Zhang Nachuan yesterday, who said that the 1.7 million yuan loan contract for Beijing City was signed on August 1st, and the funds have been delivered to the Beijing Municipal Government. It was also learned that the Beijing Municipal Government stipulated that the drainage project funds were approximately 1.1 million yuan and the water supply construction project funds were approximately 600,000 yuan, and the work has already begun separately and is expected to be completed in one year.

Salt Administration Discussion Meeting Explains the New Salt Law 97

Various sectors in this port are paying close attention to the incident of the Dai Shan fishermen's salt riot. Important organizations such as the All-Zhejiang Association have telegraphed the Zhejiang authorities, requesting lenient treatment to avoid exacerbating the situation into a major change. According to news from Beijing, the Ningbo Sojourners Association in Beijing has telegraphed the Zhejiang Provincial Government and the Two Zhejiang Salt Transport Envoy, requesting the release of the arrested fishermen. It can be seen that the people of Zhejiang are concerned about their hometown. However, the China Salt Administration Discussion Meeting believes that there are many misunderstandings about the new salt law in the Qi telegram issued by the Association, and there is a lack of understanding of the salt administration's malpractices. Therefore, it sent a letter to the Association explaining in detail. The following is an excerpt from the original letter: (Omitted above) The new salt law only has regulations for the denaturation and discoloration of salt used for industrial and agricultural purposes that are completely tax-exempt. It does not state that fishing salt should also be denatured and discolored. It is deeply aware of the fishermen's pain and should not impose harsh restrictions. Furthermore, salted fish is a food for people, and if it is made with denatured and discolored salt, it will not be welcomed by buyers. We can try to examine the imported foreign salted fish to know that fishing salt should not be denatured and discolored. As for the complicated procedures for weighing, releasing, and obtaining licenses, they are all the malpractices of the current salt officials. Their only purpose is to increase tax revenue, and they know nothing about protecting the livelihood of fishermen and competing in the international fishing industry. The state spends tens of millions of yuan to feed these ignorant salt officials, who only know how to kill and suck blood to please their superiors, which is regrettable. If the new salt law is not implemented one day, the Chinese people will not be able to live and work in peace, and Chinese society will not be able to be stable. This association has a special article on the Dai Shan tragedy and the fishing salt issue, which will be published soon. Your association is a powerful people's organization in the country, and the leaders are also outstanding people of the time. In the future, we hope that you will unanimously support the new salt law and promote its early realization to relieve the suffering of the people of the country, which is not only for the welfare of your hometown.

Danyang Silk and Satin Industry Requests Establishment of a Danyang Group Based on Precedent 101

The Silk and Satin Industry Guild will hold a meeting to discuss the inclusion of the Danyang silk industry. The industry has a long history, and the number of firms establishing branches in Shanghai is about twelve. These have already joined the Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Guild as members. However, the Silk and Satin Guild has never had a Danyang group, which has caused difficulties. Recently, due to rampant smuggling, the silk industry has been handling inventory registration and five-level procedures for transportation and sales. The Danyang silk industry, lacking affiliation, has found this especially difficult. Therefore, the twelve silk firms in the industry have jointly sent a letter to the Silk and Satin Industry Guild, requesting the establishment of a Danyang group, following the precedents of the Hangzhou Silk Group and others, to clarify the system and strengthen anti-smuggling efforts. The chairman of the Danyang County Chamber of Commerce and the chairman of the Danyang Silk Firms Industry Guild have also sent telegrams to the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce and the Silk and Satin Industry Guild, requesting special assistance. The Silk and Satin Industry Guild, after receiving the letter, will hold a meeting to discuss the matter. Details are as follows:

Letter Requesting Establishment of Danyang Group

The Danyang silk industry firms in Shanghai sent a letter to the Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Guild, stating: "To whom it may concern, Our Danyang silk industry has a long history and a renowned reputation both domestically and abroad. To facilitate business operations, we have always established branches in Shanghai, hoping to expand our business. Unexpectedly, times have changed, and smuggled goods are rampant. Therefore, we have sought to closely organize ourselves, hoping to remedy the situation to some extent. All our fellow traders are pained by the entire economic crisis and unanimously volunteered to join your guild, hoping to standardize our procedures and unite as one. After joining, we were grateful to be assigned to the Shengjing Group by your guild. All our fellow traders have complied with your guild's instructions, filled out guarantees and other documents according to the regulations, and joined the Shengjing Group. However, unexpectedly, we were rejected, leaving all our fellow traders at a loss, not knowing what to do. However, after reviewing our past, our history is quite long, and we have always been independent, clearly distinct from the Hangzhou Silk Group, the Suzhou Satin Group, and the Shengjing Group, each being unrelated to the others. If we are forced to join the Shengjing Group, not only would we be incompatible, but in fact, there would be many obstacles in the future. To avoid future disputes, we hereby invoke the precedents of your guild's Hangzhou Silk Group, Suzhou Satin Group, and others. All our fellow traders have unanimously resolved to establish a Danyang Group to clarify the system, hoping to pool our efforts to strictly combat smuggling and achieve our initial goal. For this reason, we submit the above-mentioned reasons and facts, hoping for your approval and guidance in all matters. Furthermore, before the formal establishment of the Danyang Group, we would like to know where we should have our inventories of goods registered and certified by each of our firms. We would be most grateful for your reply. Sincerely, the Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Guild Standing Committee, from all Danyang traders, Lun Chang Shen Jin Ji, Da Lun Chang, Jin Yu Heng, Da Yuan Yong Kang Ming Yuan Yi Tian Lun Ming Xing Mei Lun Tian Lai Jiu Da Yu, etc."

Telegram to the Chamber of Commerce Requesting Assistance

To Wang, Chairman of the Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Our guild members, the silk firm industry guild representatives, claim that our fellow traders have always dealt in domestic silk crepe and also engage in the artificial silk textile business. There are twelve firms, including Da Lun Chang, etc., who have joined the Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Guild as members. We have recently telegraphed the guild, requesting that the goods stored in Shanghai branches be allowed to be reported to the Customs for registration. We now telegraph again to request your special assistance to facilitate this and forward this information to the Silk and Satin Industry Guild for implementation. We eagerly await your response. Guo Songru, Chairman of the Danyang County Chamber of Commerce, respectfully.

Telegram to the Silk and Satin Industry Guild

To the Shanghai Silk and Satin Industry Guild, our fellow traders have always dealt in domestic silk crepe and also engage in the artificial silk textile business. There are twelve firms, including Da Lun Chang, etc., who have joined your guild as members. Because our fellow traders lack organization, we earnestly request that your guild provide special convenience to establish a separate group and allow all goods stored in Shanghai branches to be registered in order to facilitate transportation and sales, alleviating the difficulties of Suzhou merchants. We eagerly await your response. Zhou Lianbo, Chairman of the Danyang Silk Firms Industry Guild.

Eurasia Aviation Corporation to Offer Passenger Insurance 102

It is reported that Eurasia Aviation Corporation, in view of its five years of operation and the fact that its main routes are all in the northwest and southwest regions, areas of high mountains and deep valleys inaccessible to ships and trains, coupled with the company's use of well-manufactured and safe aircraft and its experienced and cautious pilots, has, in the five years since its founding, occasionally been forced to land due to adverse weather conditions, but without passenger injuries or fatalities, thus gaining the trust of the public, and the number of passengers has gradually increased. However, compared with the number of air passengers in Europe and the United States, the difference is still too great. It is now learned that the company, in order to further strengthen public confidence and promote the development of the aviation industry, has recently planned to offer compulsory passenger insurance, with the amount insured temporarily set at 10,000 yuan per person, and the insurance premiums will be borne by the company and will not be added to the ticket prices. Negotiations are currently underway with various domestic and foreign insurance companies, and if progress is smooth, it could be implemented next month. Once this is accomplished, it can be concluded that the number of air passengers will definitely increase by leaps and bounds, and not only will the company's business prospects be bright, but the future of the national aviation industry will also be full of infinite hope.

First Special Court to Convene Tomorrow Creditors' Meeting for Tongyi to Elect Supervisors to Oversee Bankruptcy Proceedings 104

According to the Central News Agency, Tongyi Trust Company has been closed for nearly three months. Chairman Huang Suchu has avoided appearing, and despite repeated mediation by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, there has been no practical solution. Concerned about their legal interests, creditors have successively engaged lawyers Zhang Shizhao, Zhang Yifan, Chen Changteng, and accountant Ma Qichang to file lawsuits. After multiple court hearings, a verdict is scheduled to be announced on the 18th. The First Special District Court has also approved the request of some creditors for a ruling to execute bankruptcy and will convene the first creditors' meeting tomorrow morning. In order to understand the truth, the reporter visited the Jianping Law and Accounting Firm to inquire with Lawyer Zhang, but as Zhang was out of town, accountant Ma and Lawyer Zhang Yifan received the reporter. Accountant Ma gave the following answers:

Reasons for Failure

The reporter first inquired about the reasons for the failure of Tongyi Company. It was said that although the company had a long history, it had been empty in recent years. The reasons for its failure are roughly as follows: (1) According to my statistics, the interest rate on fixed deposits in the company was generally between 9.1% and as high as 1.2%, while the loans it issued were only 1.2%. In comparison, there was not only no profit to be made, but even expenses became a problem. (2) The company's loans of 978,000 yuan to the Tongcheng Yarn Factory in Changzhou and the 300,000 yuan borrowed from the Ministry of Finance of the former Beijing government had long become bad debts, but the company still listed them as full assets. Moreover, there was no depreciation item for the company's movable assets. Therefore, although there were profits on the books in earlier years, the actual losses were considerable. (3) As mentioned above, the internal emptiness is self-evident, and the repeated issuance of dividends and bonuses over the years was all drawn from the capital account in an attempt to prolong its life. The amount withdrawn from the principal over the years reached 100,000. This policy was tantamount to accelerating its demise, so it ultimately suffered a complete and irreversible defeat.

Responsibilities of Directors and Supervisors

Regarding the question of whether creditors' deposits can be fully recovered after the company is declared bankrupt and the responsibilities of the company's directors and supervisors, it was said that regarding savings deposits, according to Article 15 of the Savings Bank Law, directors and supervisors shall bear joint and several liability for repayment, and the Ministry of Finance also has an approval, so there is no problem. Even ordinary depositors must bear joint and several liability. Although there is the title of managing director in company law, there is no provision for ordinary directors in law. According to precedent, even if directors divide their powers and manage their affairs separately, they are ultimately a single entity externally. Therefore, the directors and supervisors of the company cannot disclaim responsibility by claiming that they were not involved. Moreover, the company's collapse this time violated the provisions of Articles 231 to 233 of the Company Law's penalty clauses and should be liable for compensation to creditors in accordance with regulations. The creditors' meeting to be convened by the First Special Court on the 15th is to elect one or more supervisors to oversee the bankruptcy proceedings and effectively protect the legal interests of creditors.

Executive Yuan Revises Regulations on the Management of Civil Aviation 105

Change to Re-Register with the Nearest Customs Office The Ministries of Finance and Communications previously stipulated in Article 5 of the Regulations on Customs Management of Maritime Civilian Ships and Shipping that "All registered maritime civilian ships shall be re-registered with the original registering customs office in January of each year." For civilian ships, only re-registration with the original registering customs office was allowed, and other customs offices were not allowed to handle registration procedures, which was indeed difficult. Therefore, suggestions were drafted and submitted to the Executive Yuan to change the phrase "re-register with the original registering customs office" to "re-register with the nearest customs office or customs post." After receiving the submission, the Executive Yuan has recently approved its implementation.

Jianghai Customs to Establish Special Office for Transportation and Sales Licenses 106

The Commissioner of the Jianghai Customs stated that in accordance with the Provisional Measures for Inspecting Imported Goods, 26 kinds of foreign goods, such as rayon, and similar genuine domestic goods, require transportation and sales licenses for transportation, which is a very heavy task. Therefore, a special office for transportation and sales licenses has been established in the customs to exclusively manage the issuance of transportation and sales licenses. Merchants applying for the aforementioned licenses can contact the office.

Municipal Fishery Association Requests Clarification of National Representative Quota 107

The Shanghai Municipal Fishery Association stated that with the election of National Representatives approaching, according to the provisions of Appendix 3 of the Election Law, the Shanghai Municipal Farmers' Association and Fishery Association together have four representatives. However, the number of representatives specifically for the Fishery Association has not yet been determined. Yesterday, they specifically submitted a request to the Shanghai Election Office of the National Assembly for clarification. The original request is transcribed as follows: Request for clarification of the number of representatives from the Municipal Fishery Association and the method of selecting candidates for Fishery Association representatives in order to emphasize electoral affairs. It is noted that for this National Assembly, the Shanghai Municipal Farmers' Association and Fishery Association have a total of four representatives. Shanghai is the hub for the collection and distribution of fisheries nationwide and the only base for modern fisheries in the country. Although the number of Fishery Association members is not as large as that of the Farmers' Association, its position is no less important than that of the Farmers' Association. The number of representatives should be equally divided. However, there is no explicit provision on how many representatives each Farmers' Association and Fishery Association should have. This is the first point to be clarified. Furthermore, the Farmers' Association and Fishery Association are two professional organizations with different natures, conflicting interests, and equal status, not subordinate to each other. According to Article 20 of the National Assembly Election Law, the Farmers' Association and Fishery Association should each select candidates separately through the executive organs of the two organizations, rather than through a mixed selection. However, it has not been revealed which method will be used, leaving us at a loss. This is the second point to be clarified. The above two points are crucial to the timing of the election, and therefore we submit this document for your review and prompt instruction.

Coffin of Wu Xingya Arrives This Morning Docked at the Sanbei Company Wharf Moved to the China Funeral Home Today the Entire City Flies Flags at Half-Mast in Mourning 108

The coffin of the late Central Committee member Wu Xingya, escorted eastward by the Chang'an ship dispatched by the Military Affairs Commission, passed through Zhenjiang yesterday and is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at 10:00 AM today, docking at Berth 3 of the Sanbei Company at No. 16 Pier. The funeral committee has notified all sectors to hold a ceremony to receive the coffin, and the entire city will fly flags at half-mast in mourning. Starting tomorrow (the 15th), all sectors will take turns to hold public memorial services at the China Funeral Home. Details are as follows:

All Sectors Welcome the Coffin

At 10:00 AM today, all sectors will gather at Berth 3 of the Sanbei Company at No. 16 Pier. Participants include representatives from the Party, government, military, police, agriculture, industry, commerce, and education. The estimated number of people is around 6,000 to 7,000.

Funeral Committee Meeting

Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM, the funeral committee held a meeting of the heads of various groups and staff members at the Municipal Party Headquarters meeting room. Lu Jingshi, Jiang Huaisu, Cai Jinjun, Li Dachao, Li Suixian, Zhang Binghui, Xu Yefu, Gu Shaoyan, Hu Tianseng, Wang Jiashu, Du Mengsen, and others attended. The following key cases were resolved: (1) Command will be the responsibility of the Public Security Bureau. (2) Security will be the responsibility of the security group. (3) Re-arrange the route. (4) Pass the coffin transfer ceremony. (5) Issue black gauze paper flowers and souvenirs, which will be the responsibility of the reception group. (6) Order of precedence. The meeting adjourned after discussion.

Wharf Arrangement

Regarding the arrangement matters, Xu Yefu, the director of the arrangement group of the funeral committee, dispatched personnel to be responsible. The preparations were completed last night. The location is at the gate of the third pier of Sanbei Company at No. 16 Pier. There is a plain-colored archway with a white cloth banner hanging on it, which reads "Respectfully Welcome Mr. Wu Xingya's Coffin." Next to it is a temporary office and reception area for the funeral committee. A sacrificial platform is set up on the pier, with sacrificial tables and incense, flowers, and sacrificial offerings.

Designated Officials

Chen Lifu, Wu Tiecheng, Yang Xiaotian, Wu Kaixian, and Pan Gongzhan will be the chief officiants. Cai Jinjun, Lu Jingshi, Jiang Huaisu, Li Dachao, Li Suixian, Zhang Binghui, and Xu Yefu will be the assistant officiants. Xu Yefu will be the master of ceremonies. Representatives from youth groups and various sectors will participate in the memorial service. Zhang Binghui, director of the reception group, will be responsible for the reception arrangements.

Coffin Transfer Ceremony

The coffin transfer ceremony is as follows: (1) All stand at attention. (2) Play mourning music. (3) Transfer the coffin (youth groups). (4) Chief and assistant officiants take their places. (5) Bow three times to Mr. Wu Xingya's coffin. (6) Observe three minutes of silence in mourning. (7) Present flowers. (8) Play mourning music. (9) Ceremony concludes.

Order of Precedence

(1) Headquarters Band, (2) Military Police, (3) Self-Defense Corps, (4) Boy Scouts, (5) Youth Groups, (6) Social and Cultural Organizations, (7) Labor Sector, (8) Agricultural Sector, (9) Commercial Sector, (10) District Party Members, (11) Representatives from Various Agencies, (12) Chief and Assistant Officiants and Various Committee Members, (13) Public Security Bureau Band, (14) Coffin, (15) Family Members, (16) Police Squad.

Revised Route

The coffin transfer route will start from Berth 3 of the Sanbei Company at No. 16 Pier, then proceed along East Gate Road, Xiaodongmen, Minguo Road, cross Xinkai River, Xinbeimen, Laobeimen, Dongxin Bridge, Xiaobeimen, Fangbang Bridge, to Laoximen, then along Heben Road, enter Lafayette Road, turn into Baojian Road, to Shanzhong Road, Haige Road, and enter the China Funeral Home.

Rotating Public Memorial Services

Family Members Welcome

Five Provinces Contribute Capital to Vegetable Oil Plant Actively Proceeding with Plant Construction 109

According to the Central News Agency, in order to improve the production and manufacturing of tung oil and promote the development of foreign trade, the Ministry of Industry is organizing the establishment of a vegetable oil plant. The participating provinces include Zhejiang, Sichuan, Hunan, Hubei, and Guangxi. The authorized capital is 2 million yuan, with the Ministry of Industry responsible for 500,000 yuan, and the remaining 1.5 million yuan to be borne equally by the five provinces, with each contributing 300,000 yuan. A preparatory office was established, and Zhang Jiazhu and others were assigned to be responsible for carrying out the work. The office first dispatched experts such as Lin Tianji to visit various provinces to investigate opinions from all parties, the trends in the oil industry, and technical improvements. They have successively returned to Shanghai and drafted reports. It is reported that most of the capital to be paid by the provinces has been remitted. Zhang then took the report and went to Nanjing a few days ago and proceeded to Guling to attend the inaugural meeting to be held on the 15th. At that time, directors, supervisors, and general managers will be elected to actively proceed with the plant construction. It is reported that the main plant will be specially set up in Hankou, and several branch plants will be established in various provinces.

Case of President Wang and Others Transferred for Disciplinary Action: Xu Yongzuo's Statement: Public Announcement Within Three Days After Ruling, Stating No Violation or Disobedience 111

The Control Yuan, based on the complaint from the Shanghai Branch of Xiamen Commercial Bank, accusing Wang Simao, President of the Shanghai Second Special District Court, and Judge Tu Shenjie of illegally protecting the Funing Shipping Company liquidation case, and the impeachment document from the Jiangsu Supervisory Envoy, the review report of the supervisory committee, and the transfer document for disciplinary action from the Control Yuan, have all been published in previous reports. The liquidator appointed by the court in the liquidation case is accountant Xu Yongzuo. Accountant Xu, due to statements in the impeachment and review reports that the liquidator did not publish the announcement in the newspaper until three months after the statutory period, which may have caused losses to creditors, specifically submitted a letter to the court yesterday explaining everything. Here is the letter he sent to the court:

"Today, I read in the newspaper that Xiamen Bank has filed a complaint with the Control Yuan against President Wang and Judge Tu of the Second Special Court for illegally protecting the liquidation of the Funing Shipping Company. After investigation by the Jiangsu Supervisory Envoy, an impeachment was proposed. The main points of the impeachment are: firstly, delaying the revocation of the detention of ships; secondly, the appointed liquidator did not publish the announcement in the newspaper until three months after the statutory period, which may have caused losses to creditors and failure to fulfill supervisory responsibilities. Except for the first point, which is not related to Yongzuo, the second point is quite impossible to ignore in terms of facts and laws.

In terms of facts, Yongzuo was appointed as the liquidator in this case by a ruling on August 10, 1935. However, Yongzuo received the appointment notice on August 21st and took office on August 22nd. On that day, he immediately sent a letter to the former liquidator, Lawyer Sun Zhongyao, requesting a handover. The next day, he received a reply stating that the company's assets had already been transferred to the creditor representative, Xiamen Bank, etc., and that an objection had been filed against the Second Special Court's ruling on August 10th in accordance with the law. Therefore, on August 24th, he reported the situation to your court for instructions on whether to continue to execute the original ruling. If the original ruling was to be executed, how should the assets be retrieved? Before receiving approval, it was naturally impossible to proceed.

On November 16th, the lawyer representing the company's shareholders, Chen Yongyuan, etc., Su Fuchou, sent a letter with the second ruling on the 13th of the same month, still removing Sun Zhongyao from his position as liquidator and appointing Yongzuo as the liquidator. Therefore, on the 17th, a public announcement was drafted and sent to various newspapers for publication on the 18th. It seems to have been extremely prompt to issue the announcement within three days of receiving the second ruling. Even if calculated from the date of receiving the first ruling, it did not exceed three months. Moreover, the reason for the temporary postponement of the announcement was that the former liquidator filed an appeal and refused to hand over the assets, so it was necessary to wait for instructions on how to handle the matter. How can this be called a delay?

In terms of law, the current Company Law Article 214 applies the provisions of Article 62, which states that after the liquidator is appointed, he should use public announcement to urge creditors to report their claims, etc. There is no time limit of several months. The impeachment document states that it exceeded the statutory period of three months. The so-called statutory period is unknown.

In summary, Yongzuo, in handling this case, did not delay in fact, and did not violate the law. Even your court is not suspected of failing to fulfill its supervisory duties. However, since the original texts of the impeachment review, etc., have been disclosed in detail in the newspapers, it is inevitable that the audience will feel that your court has indeed been negligent in supervision, and that Yongzuo has indeed been negligent in his duties, which is regrettable. Yongzuo has always handled cases with a deep sense of self-respect and would never dare to neglect his duties or accept any protection, seeking to avoid all criticism. Now he is associated with your court, so he has to explain everything in detail in the hope that it will be investigated."

Domestically Produced Alcohol: Reduced Freight Rates 112

The Ministry of Railways instructed all national railway bureaus:

"According to the China Alcohol Manufacturing Co., Ltd.'s request to reduce alcohol freight rates to promote and expand sales, the Ministry has determined that alcohol is a major raw material in the chemical industry. At a time when the promotion of domestically produced chemical industrial products is encouraged, it is necessary to provide assistance. A special price for domestically produced alcohol is now set, reducing the fee by 10% based on the original grade of the alcohol. This is publicly applicable and will be implemented from August 20th of this year for a period of one year. In addition to the instructions, the order is hereby issued for compliance. This order."

Cantonese Gang: Guangxing Bank Suspended Operations Yesterday; Affected by Market Decline and Shanghai-Guangdong Exchange Rates; Liabilities of Several Tens of Thousands of Dollars; Liquidation Has Begun 113

Guangxing Bank, a Cantonese gang bank located at 553 Sichuan Road, whose main business was Shanghai-Guangdong exchange, and also engaged in money exchange business, ceased operations yesterday. A notice stating "Clearing accounts, temporarily suspending business" was posted at the entrance. A reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency learned from the money exchange industry yesterday that the bank had a capital of approximately 20,000 yuan and had been in operation for two years. It has been affected by the sluggish market, coupled with the sharp drop in Shanghai-Guangdong exchange rates, resulting in inflexible turnover and forced closure. It is currently being liquidated independently, and the total debt is said to be approximately 20,000 yuan, which is unrelated to the overall financial situation.

Telephone Problem Committee Criticizes Telephone Company: Inaccurate Counting; Requested Correction Based on Report 114

The Special District Telephone Problem Committee of this city sent a letter to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Public Concession yesterday, stating:

"Respectfully, according to a letter from Jiang Xinzhao of the Zhongping Law Firm, since the telephone company in the concessions of this city changed its charging regulations, the company's manual recording of users' call counts has been full of errors. Many users have requested reforms, but no satisfactory solution has been reached. Due to the firm's busy business and frequent calls, in order to calculate accurately, the telephone was locked immediately after the change of regulations, and a specialist was appointed to manage it and record the number of calls. Unfortunately, the monthly bills issued by the company are inconsistent with the firm's own records, and the fees charged exceed the actual number of calls. In May, there were ten extra calls, and in June, there were as many as thirty extra calls. There were also three extra calls in the Chinese area, and the July bill again had fourteen extra calls. The firm previously sent a letter to the company to investigate and correct the errors, or to provide a copy of the daily call number for verification, as it was unwilling to bear extra fees that should not be paid. However, the company's reply not only refused to correct the errors, but also refused to provide a record of the call content, only urging payment and forcing people to fulfill obligations that should not be fulfilled, which is extremely infuriating.

Telephones are public transportation tools for citizens and are originally intended to facilitate citizens. Users paying fees according to the new regulations already feel that the burden has increased. Now, the company uses illegal counting to force users to pay for calls beyond the actual number of calls; otherwise, it threatens to cut off the line. This kind of behavior should not be used by public utilities with a monopolistic nature. If it is not seriously stopped, the losses to citizens will be unimaginable. Therefore, we dare to submit this letter, respectfully requesting that the Taxpayers' Association forward it to the Public Works Department for a thorough investigation. In addition to refunding the overpayments made by each user each month, measures should be taken to strictly prevent the same mistakes from happening in the future. Otherwise, we telephone users should also rise up and strive for effective countermeasures. Your association leads users, engages in just movements, and is enthusiastic about public welfare, which we have always admired. We hope you will forward this letter as requested."

The committee agreed that the Shanghai Telephone Company's inaccurate counting has caused widespread complaints. The committee has repeatedly sent letters requesting negotiations, but the company has failed to conduct research, causing citizens to suffer unnecessary sacrifices. This kind of immoral behavior should be strictly stopped immediately. Therefore, we are forwarding this letter again, urging you to bring it up with the Public Works Department for serious negotiations as soon as possible, to prevent the same incidents from happening again in the future, and to review the company's income at any time to see if it exceeds the official interest rate of one point, so that a reduction in fees can be proposed. The matter concerns the public interest of citizens, and we hope you will speak out for justice and correct the situation, for which we will be extremely grateful.

Recently, believing that the situation had calmed down, he secretly came to Shanghai. Woman Attempts Suicide at the Bund Beijing Wharf: Only Seventeen or Eighteen Years Old, Bobbed Hair and Fashionably Dressed; Rescued and Sent to Guangci Hospital 118

Yesterday at 4:50 PM, a young woman, only seventeen or eighteen years old, suddenly appeared at the Beijing Wharf opposite the French Bund, Dama Road. She wandered around the wharf, and before long, she suddenly jumped into the Huangpu River to kill herself. At that time, there were many people standing idle on the wharf, and they shouted for help in alarm. Because she had swallowed a lot of water, she could not speak. The responsible Da Zi Ming Zhong Police Station immediately carried her onto an ambulance and sent her to Albert Road Guangci Hospital for treatment. The woman who attempted suicide was wearing a black Indian silk short shirt and pants, had bobbed hair, and her face was quite beautiful. It is not known why she committed suicide.

Chen Yinhe, a native of Haimen, 26 years old, lived at 5 Yangjia Lane, Caojiadu. He was an employee at a certain oil factory. Yesterday evening at 8:30 PM, he was riding his bicycle outside when he passed by the Caojiadu triangle area. Suddenly, a robber blocked his way, took out a handgun, and threatened him, robbing him of more than 20 yuan in national currency. Chen Yinhe resisted slightly, which angered the robber, who immediately fired two shots. Nearby police officers arrived after hearing the gunshots, but the robbers had already escaped without a trace. They had to send the two injured people to the hospital for treatment.

Main Culprit in the Stolen Cloth Sales, Wang Qiaogeng, Arrested; Dance Hostess Wang Fengzhen Implicated by Cohabitation 120

Baodaxiang Foreign Goods Cotton Cloth Shop at 99 Xiaodongmen Street, French Concession, recently discovered that a large amount of cotton cloth was missing from the warehouse. After the shop owner, Chai Zhifang, a Ningbo native, checked the missing quantity, it amounted to more than two hundred bolts. All of this was done by Wang Qiaogeng, a Ningbo native who managed the warehouse and delivered goods, in collusion with outsiders. It was found that he colluded with Zhang Qinrong, a Shaoxing native, a runner for the Lifeng Dye Factory at 4 Lane 52, Dalin Road, outside the West Gate, to sell the stolen cloth at a low price to Daxing Dye Factory at 1 Lane 29, Loushenfu Road, French Concession, Tongfengsen Cotton Cloth Shop at 160 Zhengjia Muqiao Street, and China Industrial Dye Factory at the Shanghai-Minhang South Extension Road in the Chinese area. After Chai Zhifang investigated and clarified the situation, he reported it to the French Concession Police, who dispatched detectives Lu Zhulin, Guo Shaorong, Wu Jiahui, etc., to arrest Zhang Qinrong on the 8th of this month. He was sent to the Second Special Court for interrogation on the first day of this week. However, the main culprit, Wang Qiaogeng, fled after hearing the news of the case. Through further investigation, the detectives found that Wang Qiaogeng had converted the stolen goods into cash and was living with a dance hostess at the Dadong Dance Hall named A Mao, also known as Fengzhen, 21 years old, a native of Ningbo. He first opened a room at the Xinxin Hotel at 309, and then Wang prepared modern furniture and rented the upstairs of Da Feng Tobacco and Paper Shop at 139 Gansu Road, Public Concession, for cohabitation. The investigating detectives, together with the Public Concession Police detectives, rushed to the upstairs of Da Feng Tobacco and Paper Shop at 139 Gansu Road at 8:00 AM yesterday. They first arrested Wang Qiaojing and dance hostess A Mao, and confiscated 180 yuan of the remaining stolen money. Wang was first taken to the French Concession Police for filing, and dance hostess A Mao was temporarily detained at the Huisi Police Station. Meanwhile, they arrested He Lin, the owner of Tongfengsen Shop at 160 Zhengjia Muqiao Street, and Xing Lianfang, the owner of Daxing Dye Factory at Laushenfu Road. Both of them had already fled after hearing the news. They also went to China Industrial Dye Factory on the Shanghai-Minhang South Extension Road with the Public Security Bureau and arrested the factory owner, Hu Zhongfu, who was sent to the Public Security Bureau for detention, pending transfer. Yesterday, the French Concession Police sent Wang Qiaogeng to the Criminal Division of the Second Special Court. Judge Wang Gangxu interrogated him. The lawyer from the Police Department requested a postponement to bring in the suspect detained by the Public Security Bureau who had received the stolen goods, so that he could be prosecuted together with Zhang Qinrong. Then, the plaintiff, Chai Zhifang, accompanied by his attorney, Xu Wufang, reported that 260 bolts of cotton cloth were found missing from the warehouse, each bolt worth 8 yuan, for a total value of 2,080 yuan, and requested that the case be handled according to law. The defendant Wang Qiaogeng confessed. The court ordered the case to be tried together with Zhang Qinrong on the 17th. The defendant was returned to custody.

Miss Huang Lijuan from Hunan Province Accuses of Seduction and Abandonment, Defendant is Kong Zuan, Young Owner of He Ren Weaving Factory, Huang Lijuan's Statement of Seduction with Tears 125

Kong Zuan, a Ningbo native and young owner of He Ren Weaving Factory on Beiler Road in the French Concession, is being sued by Huang Lijuan, a young woman from Hunan province, for seduction and subsequent abandonment after she gave birth. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Zhong Qing of the First Special District Court opened the trial and summoned them. According to Huang's accusation, she is 22 years old, originally from Changsha, and previously studied at Guanghua Tutoring School in Lizhiwan, Guangzhou. Because she aspired to be a nurse, she applied to a hospital in Hong Kong in January of the year before last to study nursing. She met the defendant Kong Zuan through a friend. Kong used the excuse that

Schools are everywhere

The scale is grand, not only to see much money, but also to broaden the way to further education, and persuaded her to come to Shanghai to study. After arriving in Shanghai with him, she stayed at the Young Women's Christian Association (YWCA). She repeatedly intended to apply to schools but was always prevented. In April of that year, she was seduced to the China Hotel and had physical relations with him. From then on, the defendant often invited her to movies, restaurants, and banquets, and proposed marriage to me. Once my chastity was violated, I urged him to hold the wedding soon, but he excused himself by saying that his father

Still needed to be persuaded

Around July and August, he suddenly said that his father could not agree and indicated that he should get out of the relationship as soon as possible, otherwise his father would cut off his financial support. He also said that his sister-in-law would act as a mediator and asked me to accept all the conditions she proposed. Later, his sister-in-law indeed delivered one thousand yuan and presented a separation agreement. I thought this was the defendant's way of dealing with his family, so I accepted the money and signed the agreement. Afterwards, Mrs. Hua of the YWCA

Saw through his trick

Came to advise me. I once confronted the defendant with Hua's words, but Kong still swore to heaven that he would never abandon me and even wrote a pledge. On October 1st of last year, I gave birth to a daughter. Kong was very happy and named her Yuying. However, because my status was uncertain, I kept urging him to get married, but he always made excuses to delay. Recently, his attitude suddenly changed, and he openly abandoned me, leaving me and my daughter helpless. After my investigation, I learned that he had already formed another family and married someone else, which shows that his previous seduction and his current abandonment were deliberate. I had

Repeatedly sent warning letters

But he ignored them, so I filed a lawsuit with the Second Special Court. After investigation, the facts of seduction and abandonment all occurred in the Public Concession, so I changed to file a lawsuit with your court, requesting a trial and punishment according to law. The defendant has not provided living expenses for several months. Daily necessities are all borrowed. There is also an elderly father and stepmother in my hometown, but I have not communicated with them for a long time," the woman said as she wept, her face like a pear blossom in the rain. The court then questioned the defendant Kong Zuan, who admitted to having

Lived with the plaintiff and had a daughter

Without denying it, but claimed that after meeting her in Hong Kong, he took pity on her loneliness and was willing to bring her to Shanghai to help with her tuition so that she could study. He had already made it clear in Hong Kong that he had a wife at home, and the plaintiff also stated that she would never be a burden. If I were truly infatuated with her, why didn't I live with her immediately after arriving in Shanghai, but waited until the day she lived at No. 6 Sichuan Lane, North Sichuan Road? The statement that the relationship occurred in the China Hotel is not true. As for her living expenses,

They were never cut off

Etc. The plaintiff's lawyer, Hu Yongde, then presented the defendant's written pledge not to abandon her and the defendant's love letters to the plaintiff as evidence. However, the defendant's lawyer, Liu Shichao, also presented the separation agreement signed by the plaintiff and the plaintiff's love letters to the defendant to counter the claim. Judge Zhong reviewed them and then returned them separately, instructing both parties to try to reconcile out of court. If they could not reach a peaceful settlement, they would be notified of the hearing date. The court adjourned after the deliberation.

Headless Female Corpse Seems to be a Prostitute, Autopsy Showed Signs of Venereal Disease, The So-Called "Stone Woman" is Not True 126

The Public Concession General Patrol House No. 320 of the West Third Road Patrol, on the afternoon of the 11th of this month at 8 o'clock, seized a black lacquer rattan box on Suzhou Road, containing a headless female corpse. It was sent to the Philan Road Autopsy Station. The First Special Court was notified, and the next morning, personnel were sent to the station to examine the corpse and found that she had been killed. This has been reported in the newspaper. Subsequently, the Municipal Council was concerned about whether the corpse was Chinese or a foreigner, so lawyer Li Zhishan represented the patrol house to the First Special Court, requesting an autopsy. Therefore, around 10 o'clock yesterday morning, forensic doctors Wei Ligong and Zhang Yan, together with Municipal Council doctor Smith, went to the Autopsy Station to dissect the corpse. As a result, it was determined that the female corpse was indeed Chinese and that she had suffered from venereal disease. She had also previously suffered from bubonic plague and applied plaster. Therefore, it was observed that the woman seemed to be a prostitute from the lower classes. Examining the injuries, there were only three or four small red spots on her left shoulder and a faint cyan-purple color on her lower right leg, but none of them were fatal. As for the so-called "stone woman," it was not true.

Obstacles Discovered at Shantou Port, Jardine Matheson Tugboat Removed, Hydrographic Survey Bureau Announced Yesterday 128

The Hydrographic Survey Bureau issued Notice No. 1925 yesterday regarding the removal of a sunken ship at the Yangtze River Estuary Shanghai Port. (1) Location: Within the 9th section of the Huangpu River, 283.5 degrees from the flag pole of the Gonghexiang Pudong Wharf, a distance of 1.5 chains (every 10 chains equals one nautical mile), approximately 112 degrees 01 minute east longitude and 31 degrees 05 minutes north latitude. (2) Explanation: The sunken ship "St. Atbliele" (i.e., the Jardine Matheson Tugboat) has been removed from the fairway. (3) Reporting Agency: Jianghai Customs Port Director. Furthermore, the Hydrographic Survey Bureau Notice No. 188 concerns the discovery of obstacles near Shantou Port. (1) Location: 5 degrees from the Chiwen Island triangulation point, a distance of 1.54 nautical miles, approximately 116 degrees 47 minutes east longitude and 23 degrees 18 minutes north latitude. (2) Explanation: Broken waves sometimes occur on the sea surface. It is reported that obstacles exist there. (2) Reporting Agency: Customs Transport Ship "Haixing".

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company North Wharf Labor Bidding, Shen Wenyuan Wins 129

The bidding for labor at the North Wharf of the state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company has been reviewed by the Ministry of Communications, the General Deputy Manager of the company, the Manager of the Wharf Management Office, the Assistant Managers, and the heads of various departments of the company. Shen Wenyuan's bid of 74.5% was deemed the most suitable. He was selected as the winning bidder. As for the alternate bidders, the bid prices offered by other bidders were too high, so they were deemed unqualified and therefore had to be left vacant. It is reported that the company has formally notified the winning bidder and has submitted a report to the Ministry. The original contractor of the wharf labor has been instructed to continue to be responsible as usual until the new contractor takes over.

Central Savings Association, Lottery Drawing as Usual Tomorrow 130

The Central Savings Association holds a lottery drawing for prizes once a month on the 15th. According to regulations, if it falls on a holiday, it will be held on the next day. Although tomorrow (the 15th) is Saturday and the banks are closed, the fifth lottery drawing of the association will still be held as usual at 2:00 PM at the Municipal Chamber of Commerce near the Tianhou Palace Bridge. The special prize is still guaranteed by the association to be 25,000 yuan. The first, second, third, and fourth prizes have each been increased to eleven. There are also many supplementary prizes and last prizes. Those who are interested in saving can still pay and join the association before 11:00 AM tomorrow. The association will issue a temporary receipt with a number on it for inclusion in this period's lottery drawing.

Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association, This Year's Budget Approved, Simplification of Election of Rickshaw Puller Directors, Last Year's Accounts Audited and Published 131

The budget of the Rickshaw Pullers Mutual Aid Association for this year, starting from August 1, has been approved by the Council through a notice, as the Council did not have a quorum last time. According to the provisions of the budget, the monthly expenditure of the Mutual Aid Association is about 15,300 yuan. This amount actually accounts for the total income of the association and all bank interest. On the expenditure side, medicine accounts for the largest portion, about a little over one-third of the total. Direct relief and insurance account for less than about 23%. Salaries, rent, water, electricity, telephone, and miscellaneous expenses account for a little over 17%. Other expenses, such as education, bathing, tea, games, license fees, etc., account for a little over a quarter of the total. In addition, regarding the election of rickshaw puller representatives to the Council, last year, the public notary selected 400 rickshaw puller voters, that is, one person was drawn from every 100 people. By the due date, the 400 people gathered to hold an election. This election procedure has been simplified as much as possible. That is, the number of units is first drawn by lottery. After the number is drawn, all rickshaw puller licenses ending in those two numbers should be the voters. For example, if the two numbers drawn are "two" and "four" together, it is "twenty-four," and the rickshaw puller license numbers ending in "twenty-four," such as "〇〇24," "〇124," "〇224," "〇324," etc., are all voters. The remaining election procedures remain the same, that is, the two people with the most votes are the rickshaw puller directors, and the next two with the most votes are the alternate directors. Furthermore, the accounts of the Mutual Aid Association for the last year up to July 31 of this year are currently being audited by an accountant. Once the audit is completed and approved by the Custody Committee, it will be published.

We believe that promoting national products and preventing economic outflow is the bounden duty of merchants and the only way to save and survive at present. Hua An Bank Case, Ye Jingliang Suspected, Detained the Day Before Yesterday, Released on Bail Yesterday 133

Fang Su'an, a Ningbo native and director of Hua An Bank at No. 73 Ningbo Road (also known as Chuanxun, the young owner of Ankang Money Shop), purchased 50,000 yuan of customs treasury bonds in June of last year. Because the market price fell, Fang colluded with Ye Jingliang, a Shanghai native and manager of Hua An Bank, to transfer the treasury bonds to the bank's account, so that the bank suffered the losses. Zhang Zhigu, a shareholder, reported this to the General Patrol House. Inspector Yang Peisheng and detective Kang Zengxiang arrested Fang and sent him to the First Special District Court. Fang's lawyer, Wu Linkun, and others argued that shareholder Ding Zhixian had previously hired lawyer Yang Ruinian to file a lawsuit with the court based on the same facts. According to the principle of non bis in idem, the case could not be prosecuted again. After the court ordered the file to be retrieved and reviewed, Fang was allowed to be released on bail by lawyer Wu and others. The details have been reported in yesterday's newspaper. The patrol house suspected that Ye Jingliang, the manager of the bank, was jointly suspected, so on the day before yesterday, the patrolman accompanied Fang Su'an to Hua An Bank and arrested Ye and took him back to the patrol house. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Criminal Division of the First Special Court. The patrol house's lawyer, Wang Yaochang, prosecuted him for embezzlement and breach of trust under Article 336, paragraph 2, and Article 342, paragraph 1 of the Criminal Law. He also stated that the case was related to Fang's plan, so he requested that the cases be heard together. Ye Jingliang confessed that the treasury bonds were originally purchased by Fang Su'an personally, and Fang repeatedly discussed it with me before transferring them to the bank's account. The purchase date of the bonds was June 10 of last year, with a loss of 593 yuan. He also hired lawyer Jiang Baoli to defend him and requested that he be allowed to be released on bail. After Judge Qian Hongye reviewed the confession, he ordered that the hearing be changed to be heard together with Fang Su'an. Ye Jingliang was allowed to be released on bail for 1,000 yuan.

Robbery at Zhen'anli Case, Six Robbers Transferred to Public Security Bureau, Geng Desheng's Public Endangerment Crime, Sentenced to Three Years in Prison First 134

At 5:10 AM on the 9th of this month, Tao Jugui's home at No. 4 Zhen'anli, Gonghe Road, Zhabei, was suddenly invaded by several armed robbers who looted clothing, banknotes, jewelry, and other items. The victim immediately reported to the Xinzhai Sub-bureau of the Public Security Bureau, which was in charge, and ordered detectives to investigate. Over the past few days, eight suspects, including Gong, have been arrested. Zhong Da, the leader of the sub-bureau, learned that Luo Zibao, a Jiangbei native and former Chinese patrolman No. 319 of the French Concession, was also involved in the case. Luo lived in a shed on Haifang Road, West Shanghai, in the Public Concession. So, at 6:00 AM the day before yesterday, Leader Zhong led detectives and worked with Zhu Mengwei, the Chinese patrol leader of the Gordon Road Patrol, to secretly arrest Luo and others. Then, in an empty house at No. 111 Mazaki Road, he continued to capture accomplices Geng Desheng, Chen Chunyang, Zhou Kaixuan (i.e., Li Debiao), and Huan Qingshui, all from Jiangbei. A Dimeng brand pistol, ten bullets, and two bullet boxes were found beside Geng Desheng. Also, Huan Xiaoliuzi, a Jiangbei native, was arrested at the intersection of Gordon Road and Changping Road. Two silver bracelets (the original stolen goods from Tao's house) were found on him. They were all taken back to the patrol house for detention. Yesterday morning, they were sent to the Eighth Criminal Division of the First Special Court. Zhang Tianyin, the patrol house lawyer, stated the above situation, saying that the patrol house was prosecuting Geng Desheng for the crime of public endangerment under Article 187 of the Criminal Law because a pistol was found beside him and he had not applied for a license from the Municipal Council. After Geng Desheng's case was concluded, he and Luo Zibao and others were transferred to the Public Security Bureau for investigation. Judge Tan Xinzhen questioned Luo Zibao and others briefly and immediately sentenced Geng Desheng to three years imprisonment for intending to use military firearms and ammunition for criminal purposes. The pistol and ten bullets were confiscated. Luo Zibao, Geng Desheng, Chen Chunyang, Zhou Kaixuan, Huan Qingshui, and Huan Xiaoliuzi were all handed over to Zheng Da, an official from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, to be taken back for investigation. The firearms, ammunition, and stolen goods were transferred together. Geng Desheng should still be sent back for execution after the interrogation.

The Sixth Day of the Li Society Painting Exhibition 135

Yesterday was the sixth day of the Li Society painting and calligraphy exhibition. In order to improve employee welfare and meet actual needs, the Ministry of Railways is planning to establish large-scale hospitals on the Pinghan, Longhai, Xiang'e, Jinghu-Hangyong, Zhegan Jinpu, and other lines. The Mountain Purchasing Committee is purchasing large amounts of hygienic medical equipment and medicines, X-rays, etc. For the beds used in the hospitals, a total of 10,000 were purchased, all of which were manufactured by the Mubu Aiduoya Siemens Bed Factory. They have now been put into production and are being transported separately for application. It is reported that the hospitals on each line will all be put into operation within the mountain. The Hongqiao Sanatorium in this area, recognizing the importance of early diagnosis of lung disease, is holding a group X-ray examination for tuberculosis prevention. This matter concerns public health and has attracted the attention of people in society. The second group examination has been scheduled for the morning of next friend at 9:00 AM. The location is still at No. 4 Daxi Road, Jing'an Temple Branch. The transportation there is extremely convenient. Its large X-ray machine has all safety equipment. Its newly shipped fluorescent screen for examination is particularly transparent. At the same time, examinees can use a reflective device to see all the movements of their own heart and lungs, as well as the location of the disease. This is especially characteristic. Those who wish to be examined, whether groups or individuals, only need to purchase a registration certificate from the Shen Bao Office in advance. According to the Medical Committee's motion of the Chinese Anti-Tuberculosis Association, the fee is only one yuan per person. Each certificate has a specified time, so that they can be checked as soon as they arrive. It is reported that the municipal government will issue an order to all schools for large-scale inspections in the near future.

A New Ghost in the Suzhou Creek, Yu Guitong Drowned While Swimming 138

Yu Guitong, a 29-year-old Huzhou native who worked as a cook in the kitchen of the Kenye Bank in this city, went to the Suzhou Creek under the Jiangxi Road Bridge at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday with five or six other cooks to swim. Yu volunteered to swim from the south bank to the north bank, but he did not reach the destination. Because he was physically exhausted, his body suddenly sank to the bottom of the river. His companions could not rescue him and rushed back to the bank to report. His brother Yu Maolin hired a net-dredging boat, and it was not until 7:00 PM that night that the body was pulled up. That night, the brother of the deceased requested the Customs Water Patrol House to waive the inspection and collected the body himself.

The other two in front of a rice store on Lafayette Road and one in front of a clock shop had been damaged for a long time, leaving only rotten coffins. As a result, passers-by stopped to watch.

If there is any violation, I am willing to accept severe punishment." The registration form must state the name, age, place of origin, occupation, level, address, and other items.

After the Stoppage of the Shengsi Survey, Jiangsu Province Actively Manages and Develops Resources as Soon as Possible 143

The dispute over the administration of the Shengsi Islands in the outer seas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang occurred when Ge Tan, the Commissioner of the Nantong District of Jiangsu, and Zhao Cisheng, the Commissioner of the Ningbo District of Zhejiang, met on June 23 to conduct a survey. However, Commissioner Zhao firmly insisted that the principle of dividing the Shengsi Islands into Zhejiang must be determined first before the survey could be conducted, resulting in no results and dispersal. Commissioner Ge believed that since the survey had no results, the government would not be able to resolve the issue in a timely manner, and the most important thing at present was to actively manage them so that resources could be developed as soon as possible. He planned to reform the local military police, education, and judicial aspects with Gu Hongxi, the magistrate of Chongming County, and agreed on fishery improvement and loan methods with the Jiangsu Provincial Fisheries Experiment Field, the Jiangsu Farmers Bank, and the Fisheries Loan Office of the Ministry of Industry. He sent a letter to the Jiangsu Provincial Government to order them to comply. The Jiangsu Construction Department has now transferred the order to the Fisheries Experiment Field to draft a detailed plan for the relocation and establishment of a factory and to report it for approval. The remaining reforms are also being transferred for implementation. The issue of the division of the Shengsi, which has been in dispute for more than a year, will likely end without a conclusion. Xu Zhishi, a native of Yixing, Jiangsu, is a diligent scholar and has always been a teacher. He graduated from the Department of Civil Engineering of Zhejiang University in 1934. He immediately worked for the Shanghai Municipal Engineering Bureau and studied and worked on all projects, large and small, with care and diligence. He is scheduled to resign on the 18th of this month and travel to the United States on the Grand President to study at Cornell University to prepare for his return to the country and contribute to society.

Weather Report 153

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that Shandong is clear and cloudy, with northeast to southeast winds. The upper and middle reaches of the Yellow River and the Yangtze River have showers and light northeast winds. The lower reaches of the Yangtze River and the East China Sea are cloudy, with the possibility of showers and strong easterly winds. The hurricane south of Hong Kong is still moving northwest-west. Its center at 2 PM was within approximately 120 miles of 21 degrees north latitude and 114 degrees east longitude. The wind force is unknown. The hurricane north of Palau Island is clearly shifting northwest. Its center at 2 PM was within approximately 120 miles of 11 degrees north latitude and 133 degrees east longitude. The wind force is also unknown. Furthermore, in the 24 hours before 3 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 93.9 degrees and the lowest was 79.2 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest was 91.8 degrees and the lowest was 75.6 degrees.

The 11th Olympic Games 1936

Basketball Championship: USA and Canada to Play Final 154

USA Team Has Tall Players and Clever Tactics; 56-23 Victory Over Philippines 155

Central News Agency Special Correspondent, Berlin, 13th: Yesterday's basketball competition, the game between the United States and the Philippines, was the most exciting. American basketball is renowned worldwide, while Philippine basketball dominates the Far East. Therefore, when these two powerhouses met, the competition was intense. The American players are tall and have seasoned tactics. After the start of the game, they took an early lead of 7-2. The Philippine team resisted tenaciously, but ultimately succumbed to the disparity in strength and remained behind. As a result, the US won the first half 28-20. In the second half, the American team became even more active. Their strict defense made it difficult for the Filipinos to cross the line. After getting the ball, they never rushed forward, but seized opportunities when they arose, catching the enemy off guard. Therefore, after the start of the second half, they scored nine consecutive points. The Philippine team's close attacks were ineffective, and their long shots were even less accurate. As a result, they lost the second half 3-22. The overall result was a decisive victory for the US with a score of 56-23. The American players are tall, and if they miss a shot, they can still jump up and put it in. When the Philippine team shoots, the ball is often intercepted by the Americans jumping up. If the shot is missed, the ball will definitely end up in the hands of the American team. As for Canada's victory over Uruguay, Uruguay is a strong team with quick movements, but the Canadian team's tactics are even more special. No matter the environment, their passing and dribbling are agile and quick, without the hesitation seen in other teams. Their defense is particularly strong, and their victory was not accidental. Yesterday's basketball results: (1) USA defeated the Philippines, 56-23; (2) Mexico defeated Italy, (3) 14-17 (first half 20-7); (3) Canada defeated Uruguay 43-21 (first half 23-6); The game between Peru and Poland was not played because Peru withdrew.

Today's schedule is football Norway vs. Poland at 5:00 PM for third and fourth place, Austria vs. Italy will be the final on the 15th, and basketball will be the United States vs. Mexico, Canada vs. Poland, and the Philippines vs. Italy. Judging from the strength of each team, the United States and Canada are the most advantageous, and the championship will be decided by the US and Canada.

World Games Torch Extinguished; Games Flag Lowered in Kiel; Sailing Competition Concludes 163

Kuomintang News Agency, August 13, Kiel: The World Games torch, which had shone here for nine days, was extinguished last night at the end of the sailing competition. During the solemn closing ceremony, the World Games flag was also slowly lowered. The German Navy, which had participated in the World Games torch relay, returned the World Games flag to Colonel Kiwiets, president of the German Maritime Association, for safekeeping. Upon receiving the flag, Colonel Kiwiets said, "I will carefully preserve this flag and will hang it high in Japan when the World Games are reopened in four years."

In a brief speech, Colonel Kiwiets stated that the medals won by athletes from various countries who participated in the World Games sailing competition would be formally awarded in Berlin. In accordance with the instructions of the World Games Committee, each winner was first given a laurel wreath as a souvenir, and then girls from Hitler's Youth Group presided over the ceremony.

Kuomintang News Agency, August 13, Kiel: The sailing competition sub-committee of the organizing committee of the 11th World Games announced here today that the scores for the Swiss 10,000-meter sailing race were deemed invalid because the helmsman lost his amateur status.
